AXIS MAX LIFE INSURANCE CO. LTD.

​Axis Max Life Insurance Limited, formerly known as Max Life Insurance Company Limited, is a prominent Indian life insurance company headquartered in New Delhi. It operates as a joint venture between Max Financial Services Limited and Axis Bank Limited, with Max Financial Services holding an 80% stake and Axis Bank holding 20%
Axis Max Life Insurance is a joint venture between:
  1. Max Financial Services Limited (MFSL): Holding an 80% stake, MFSL is part of the Max Group, an Indian multi-business corporation
  2. Axis Bank Limited: Holding a 20% stake, Axis Bank is one of India's largest private-sector banks
The collaboration between Max Life and Axis Bank evolved from a distribution partnership in 2010-11 to shared branding in 2024, reflecting a deepening strategic alliance

Key Highlights of AXIS MAX LIFE INSURANCE

  1. Established Presence:: Founded in 2001, Axis Max Life Insurance has over two decades of experience in the Indian insurance sector.​
  2. Comprehensive Product Portfolio:The company offers a wide range of insurance products, including TERM LIFE INSURANCE, UNIT-LINKED INSURANCE PLANS (ULIPs), ENDOWMENT, TRADITIONAL SAVINGS PRODUCTS, WHOLE LIFE INSURANCE, ANNUITY PRODUCTS & HEALTH INSURANCE SOLUTIONS ​

    TERM INSURANCE (PURE RISK COVER)

    A Term Insurance Plan is the simplest and purest form of life insurance.
    Mr. X pays a fixed premium every month/year, and if the insured person dies during the policy term, the insurance company pays a large amount (called SUM ASSURED) to the nominee/family.
    Term insurance is a pure life insurance product, which provides financial protection to the policyholder. In case of death of the insured during the policy period, the beneficiary receives as defined under the chosen term insurance plan. Securing your family in your absence should be your top priority and a term life insurance plan is the risk-free way to do so. Term plan ensures that the financial security of your family is maintained even after your death. Moreover, it does not affect your current lifestyle as it can be easily afforded given the coverage you’re opting for.
    Think of it as:“Income protection for your family.”
    Why Everyone Should Have a Term Plan: A term plan is important because your family may depend on your income.

    1. Family Financial Protection: If the earning member dies, the family still needs money for:

  • Daily expenses
  • Children's education
  • Home loan EMI
  • Marriage expenses
  • Medical costs

    • A term plan gives immediate financial support

    2. Very High Coverage at Low Cost: You can get:

  • ₹1 crore cover at a relatively low premium if bought young and healthy

    • This makes term insurance the most affordable life cover.
    3. Helps Repay Loans: If you have:

  • Home Loan
  • Car loan
  • Personal loan

    • The Insurance amount can help your family repay debts
    4. Tax Benefits

  • Premiums paid are eligible for tax deductions under Section 80C, and claim payouts are generally tax-free under Section 10(10D).

    • 5. Peace of Mind

  • Your family remains financially secure even in your absence.
    •

    How a Term Plan Works

    1. Choose coverage amount Example: ₹50 lakh, ₹1 crore, ₹2 crore
    2. Choose policy term Example: till age 60, 70, or 85
    3. Pay premiums Monthly, quarterly, yearly, or limited years
    4. Insurance company evaluates:
    5. Age
    6. Income
    7. Health
    8. Smoking habits
    9. Medical history

      10. 5. If insured dies during policy term: o Nominee receives claim amount
      6. If insured survives:

    10. Pure term plan → usually no maturity amount
    11. Return of Premium (ROP) plan → premiums may be returned

    Term Insurance Medical Test

    Having a term insurance plan can help you create a financial backup for your family, in case of your untimely death. In your absence, the insurance benefit from the term policy will take care of all financial needs such as your children’s education, paying back loans, and managing household bills.
    As part of the term insurance purchase process, however, you need to undergo a comprehensive term insurance medical test.
    Based on the term plan medical test results, the insurance provider will determine your overall health condition and your risk profile. features and benefits it offers.
    Subsequently, the insurer will create customized term insurance policy quotes for you, so that you can choose the term plan variant that offers maximal benefits for cost-effective premium rates.
    A medical test for term insurance may be needed based on multiple factors such as the applicant’s age, health profile as well as insurer’s internal policies such as sum assured and type of policy being offered. People with lifestyle habits, such as smoking, alcohol consumption, or other risk factors such as family history of cancer/cardiovascular diseases, etc. may need to undergo a medical test irrespective of their age.
    A medical test at the time of life insurance application helps insurers check the potential health risks and life expectancy, which can later influence the premium charged, coverage period, and sum assured offered under the policies. Individuals who are determined to be at higher risk of diseases may be charged a higher premium, be offered a lower sum assured or fulfill additional requirements as per the insurer’s policies. Similarly, in many cases, younger individuals who are opting for lower sum assured life insurance policies may receive the benefit of not having to undergo a medical test as part of the application process. In the end it all depends on the internal policies and discretion of the insurer

    Factors Affected by Term Insurance Medical Test

    The primary purpose of any term insurance medical test in India is for the insurance provider to know everything about a term plan applicant’s health. Subsequently, the insurer can proceed to create a personalized term insurance coverage – complete with maximal coverage tenure, optimal rates of premium payable and host of other policy benefits.
    The terms and conditions for life insurance plans, primarily term insurance, are determined based on the results of the term insurance medical test that the insurance company asks you to undergo. Let us look at some policy attributes that get affected by the results of a term plan medical test:

  • Premium Rates: Higher risk profiles may lead to increased premiums.
    The primary goal of the insurance provider is to calculate the amount of premium payable towards your term plan. The life insurance business model works based on the overall risk perception of an applicant.
    Therefore, the insurer must determine your existing physical health condition before they can determine what will be the appropriate quotation for the premium payable towards the plan.
    If you are in peak physical health, then your premium payable will be low. On the other hand, if the term insurance medical test identifies any pre-existing medical conditions, the risk factor associated with you becomes higher. Subsequently, you may have to pay a higher amount of premium your desired coverage.
    The possibility of a high premium amount has historically been a key detractor for Indians planning to purchase a life insurance policy.
    Now recent data from Axis Max Life IPQ 7.0 Survey has recorded a shift with the quantum of life cover gaining near equal importance among Indians planning to purchase a life insurance policy.
  • Sum Assured: Individuals at higher risk may receive a lower sum assured.
    Another aspect of the term insurance policy that is affected by the term insurance medical test results results is the sum assured.
    The Sum Assured is the amount of insurance benefit money that your family receives, in case of an unfortunate event taking place during the term policy tenure.
    The term insurance medical test can help you avail of a higher amount of Sum Assured if your results are relatively healthy. The insurance policies that do not require any medical test for term insurance in India usually offer a lower Sum Assured, which, may often prove to be inadequate in covering your family financially. On the other hand, if your term insurance medical test results indicate a higher risk profile, then the insurance provider may offer you a lower sum assured, which may not be sufficient to cover your family’s financial needs in your absence.
    The sum assured offered to you by the insurance provider is a key factor that you should consider while purchasing a term insurance policy.
    It is important to ensure that the sum assured is sufficient to cover your family’s financial needs in your absence, and the term insurance medical test results can play a crucial role in determining the sum assured offered to you.
  • Coverage Period: Some insurers may limit the coverage period for high-risk applicants.
  • CLAIM REJECTION: Many people mistakenly believe that even if they have a pre-existing health condition, they can avail the desired coverage by opting for a plan that does not require a term insurance medical test.
    At the time of claim settlement, if the insurance provider finds that the policyholder’s untimely demise is a result of any pre-existing condition that was not mentioned in their application, the insurer can reject your term insurance claim.
    Filling out your term insurance application requires you to disclose any existing health conditions which may develop into life-threatening ailments later and result in claim rejection.

    • Common Medical Tests for Term Insurance

    Here are some of the essential term plan medical tests required by insurers for term insurance

    1. Medical History Questionnaire
    2. BODY MASS INDEX (BMI): ): It is a measure that classifies an individual as underweight, overweight, obese, or healthy, based on their height and weight, to assess overall body fat composition.
    3. BLOOD PRESSURE: It is the force exerted by circulating blood on the walls of blood vessels, measured in millimetres of mercury (mmHg) and expressed as two numbers: systolic pressure (when the heart beats) over diastolic pressure (when the heart rests between beats).
    4. HEART RATE: It is the number of times the heart beats per minute (bpm), indicating cardiovascular health and fitness levels.
    5. CHOLESTEROL LEVELS: It is the measurement of the amount of cholesterol in the blood, including total cholesterol, LDL (low-density lipoprotein), HDL (high-density lipoprotein), and triglycerides, which are important indicators of cardiovascular health.
    6. PATHOLOGICAL TESTS
      • COMPLETE BLOOD COUNT (CBC): It measures several blood components to provide an overview of overall health. This test is part of routine health check-ups as it helps diagnose various symptoms, followed by necessary treatment
      • BLOOD GLUCOSE TEST: Measures glucose levels in blood.
      • LIPID PROFILE: Measures the levels of different fats in the blood, including cholesterol and triglycerides.
      • LIVER FUNCTION TEST (LFT): Evaluates the health of the liver by measuring levels of enzymes, proteins, and bilirubin in the blood.
      • KIDNEY FUNCTION TEST (KFT): Assesses kidney health by measuring levels of creatinine, urea, and electrolytes in the blood.
      • URINE ROUTINE TEST (URT): Evaluates kidney function and detects urinary tract infections or other kidney-related issues.
    7. Specialised Tests
      • ECG (ELECTROCARDIOGRAM): Records the electrical activity of the heart to detect any abnormalities.
      • CHEST X-RAY: Provides images of the chest to evaluate lung and heart health.
      • ECHOCARDIOGRAPHY: A detailed analysis of the heart function
      • ULTRASOUND: Uses sound waves to create images of internal organs, such as the abdomen or pelvis, to assess their health.
      • ULTRASONOGRAPHY: Examination of the internal organs to confirm suspected health conditions.

    SMART TERM with ADDITIONAL RETURNS (STAR) ULIP

    PRODUCT KEY FEATURES

    The STAR Term Plan by Axis Max Life Insurance, officially known as the Smart Term with Additional Returns (STAR) ULIP, is a Unit Linked Insurance Plan that combines life insurance coverage with investment opportunities. It is designed to provide both financial protection and wealth creation, making it suitable for individuals seeking comprehensive financial planning. This Unit Linked Insurance Plan (ULIP) offers policyholders the flexibility to tailor their investment strategies while ensuring financial security for their families.

    Dual Benefit: Protection and Investment

    Life Insurance Coverage Offers a high sum assured, up to 215 times the annualized premium, providing substantial financial protection to your beneficiaries in case of unforeseen events
    Wealth Creation: Invests in market-linked funds, allowing your investments to grow over time based on market performance.

    Plan Variants

    Life Secure Variant: Provides a lump-sum death benefit along with the maturity benefit of the total fund value
    3D Life Secure Variant In addition to the benefits of the Life Secure Variant, Comprehensive Shield with 3D Life Secure Variant. This variant offers protection against death, critical illness, and dismemberment, ensuring a holistic safety net for the insured and their family as it offers:
    1. Monthly income payouts of 20% of the base annualized premium for 10 years.
    2. Funding of up to 3 times the future premiums in case of death, critical illness, or dismemberment
    Flexible Investment Options Choose from a variety of market-linked funds to align with your financial goals and risk appetite

    Additional Riders for Enhanced Protection

    Optional Riders Enhance your coverage by adding riders such as Accidental Death Benefit, Critical Illness, and Waiver of Premium, providing extra layers of financial security
    Critical Illness and Disability Rider Provides coverage against 64 critical illnesses and permanent disability
    Waiver of Premium Plus Rider Waives all future premiums in case of critical illness, dismemberment, or death
    Accidental Death and Dismemberment Rider Offers additional protection in case of accidental death or disability.
    Smart Withdrawal Functionality Available in the Whole Life option, this feature allows for monthly income withdrawals, offering liquidity during the policy term
    Wealth Creation Through Market-Linked Returns Policyholders can invest in a variety of market-linked funds, aligning the plan with their financial goals and risk tolerance.
    Flexible Premium Payment Options The plan provides various premium ayment options, allowing policyholders to choose a payment structure that best fits their financial planning.

    SMART TERM PLAN PLUS (STPP)

    The STPP Term Plan by Axis Max Life Insurance, officially known as the Smart Term Plan Plus (STPP), is a comprehensive term insurance solution designed to offer flexible and customizable protection to meet diverse financial needs.
    STPP offers 7 distinct plan variants, allowing policyholders to choose coverage that aligns with their specific requirements
    KEY FEATURES

  • Flexibility to choose from 6 plan variants based on your needs

    2. Lifeline Plus: Flexibility to avail Top-up in the event of the death of the spouse of female Lifeinsured
    STPP offers 7 distinct plan variants, allowing policyholders to choose coverage that aligns with their specific requirements

    REGULAR COVER The Base Sum Assured chosen at inception remains level throughout the policy term. In case life assured dies during the policy term, the Guaranteed Death benefit shall be payable, and the policy will terminate
    REBALANCING COVER Initially allocates 10% of the sum assured to life cover and 90% to accidental death benefit, with annual adjustments until the entire sum assured becomes life cover
    EARLY RETURN OF PREMIUM (ROP) On survival of the life insured, the policyholder will get back 50% of the total premiums paid (plus underwriting extra premiums paid plus loading for modal premiums, if any) on higher of (on attainment of age 60 or Age at entry + Premium Payment Term + 10) and yet, continue the life cover with 50% of Base Sum Assured till the end of Policy term.
    The remaining 50% of the total premiums paid (plus underwriting extra premiums paid plus loading for modal premiums, if any) shall be paid back at the end of policy term, in case of survival of Life insured till the end of policy term
    In case of death of life assured during the policy term, provided all due premiums have been paid, the applicable Guaranteed Death benefit shall be payable.
    Returns 50% of total premiums paid at a specified milestone, with the remaining 50% returned at the end of the policy term, while maintaining life cover throughout
    SMART COVER Offers 150% of the base sum assured in case of death within the first 15 policy years, and 100% thereafter.
    RETURN OF PREMIUM The Base Sum Assured chosen at inception will remain level throughout the term of the policy.
    In case life assured dies during the policy term, the Guaranteed Death benefit shall be payable, and policy terminates thereafter.
    In case of survival of life insured till the end of policy term, 100% of the total premiums paid (plus underwriting extra premiums paid plus loading for modal premiums, if any) will be payable Refunds 100% of total premiums paid upon survival till the end of the policy term
    WHOLE LIFE COVER Provides coverage up to 100 years of age, with partial premium returns at specified milestones.
    INCOME PROTECTION COVER Under this plan variant, in case of death of the life assured during the policy term, provided the policy is in force, the Guaranteed Death benefit will be payable in the form of ‘monthly income applicable at the time of death, commencing from the end of the policy month on or after the date of intimation of death and continue for each policy month till the higher of 120 months or the outstanding term in months. Where the outstanding term in months is equal to the number of whole months from the date of death to the end of the Policy Term.
    The policyholder will have the choice to opt for either ‘Level Income’ or ‘Inflation-proof Income’ options.
    The ‘monthly income applicable at the time of death’ will depend on the option chosen by the policyholder and the same has been Delivers monthly income to beneficiaries in the event of the policyholder's death, with options for level or inflation-adjusted payouts

    PLAN VARIANTS KEY FEATURES
    Regular Cover The Base Sum Assured chosen at inception remains level throughout the policy term. In case life assured dies during the policy term, the Guaranteed Death benefit shall be payable, and the policy will terminate.
    FEATURES
    1. What it does: Simple level life cover— base Sum Assured remains the same throughout the policy term; on death the lump-sum Sum Assured is paid and policy terminates.
    2. Useful when: You want a traditional term plan with straightforward lump-sum protection
    Rebalancing Cover Initially allocates 10% of the sum assured to life cover and 90% to accidental death benefit, with annual adjustments until the entire sum assured becomes life cover.​
    FEATURES
    1. What it does: Splits the Base Sum Assured into a Life Cover SA and an Accidental Death Benefit (ADB) SA. At inception Life SA starts low (e.g., 10%) and ADB high (e.g., 90%); every policy anniversary Life SA increases by a fixed amount (10% of base SA simple interest) while ADB decreases by the same amount.
      — effectively rebalancing accidental vs non-accidental protection over time.
    2. Useful when: You want higher accidental cover initially (e.g., for younger working years) that progressively shifts toward regular life cover later
    Early Return of Premium (ROP) Plus On survival of the life insured, the policyholder will get back 50% of the total premiums paid (plus underwriting extra premiums paid plus loading for modal premiums, if any) on higher of (on attainment of age 60 or Age at entry + Premium Payment Term + 10) and yet, continue the life cover with 50% of Base Sum Assured till the end of Policy term.
    The remaining 50% of the total premiums paid (plus underwriting extra premiums paid plus loading for modal premiums, if any) shall be paid back at the end of policy term, in case of survival of Life insured till the end of policy term
    In case of death of life assured during the policy term, provided all due premiums have been paid, the applicable Guaranteed Death benefit shall be payable. Returns 50% of total premiums paid at a specified milestone, with the remaining 50% returned at the end of the policy term, while maintaining life cover throughout.
    FEATURES
    1. What it does: On survival to a specified milestone age (whichever is higher of attainment of age 60 or entry age + PPT + 10), the policy returns 50% of total premiums paid and continues with 50% of base sum assured for the remaining term; the remaining 50% of premiums is paid back at final maturity. (Full details depend on chosen PPT and policy term.)
    2. Useful when: You want a mix of term cover plus partial early recovery of premiums (helps those wanting mid-life liquidity or lower cover later).
    Smart Cover Offers 150% of the base sum assured in case of death within the first 15 policy years, and 100% thereafter.
    FEATURES
    1. What it does:Higher cover in early years — 150% of base Sum Assured is payable if death occurs within the first 15 policy years; thereafter 100% of base SA applies.
    2. Useful when: You need extra protection in the initial phase (e.g., while you have large liabilities such as a home loan or young dependents). Note: Regular pay may not be available in this variant (check PPT restrictions).
    Return of Premium The Base Sum Assured chosen at inception will remain level throughout the term of the policy. In case life assured dies during the policy term, the Guaranteed Death benefit shall be payable, and policy terminates thereafter.
    In case of survival of life insured till the end of policy term, 100% of the total premiums paid (plus underwriting extra premiums paid plus loading for modal premiums, if any) will be payable
    Refunds 100% of total premiums paid upon survival till the end of the policy term.
    FEATURES
    1. What it does:If the Life Insured survives the policy term, 100% of total premiums paid (plus any underwriting extra and modal loadings) are returned at maturity.
      On death during the term the base Sum Assured is paid and policy terminates.
    2. Useful when:You prefer a term policy but want your premiums refunded if you outlive the cover (higher cost vs plain term
    Whole Life Cover Provides coverage up to 100 years of age, with partial premium returns at specified milestones.
    FEATURES
    1. What it does:Gives lifecycle options — on survival to a specified milestone (similar to Early ROP rules) the policy pays back 50% of premiums and continues life cover at 50% of base SA till the end of the policy; the remaining 50% of premiums are payable at age 100 when the policy then terminates.
      Death benefit rules and continued cover differ from conventional term plans this variant provides life cover up to advanced ages. .
    2. Useful when: You want long-term/whole-life style protection (cover beyond standard term) plus return of part of premiums at milestones
    Income Protection Cover Under this plan variant, in case of death of life assured during the policy term, provided the policy is in force, the Guaranteed Death benefit will be payable in the form of ‘monthly income applicable at the time of death, commencing from the end of the policy month on or after the date of intimation of death and continue for each policy month till the higher of 120 months or the outstanding term in months.
    Where the outstanding term in months is equal to the number of whole months from the date of death to the end of the Policy Term.
    The policyholder will have the choice to opt for either ‘Level Income’ or ‘Inflation proofIncome’ options.
    The ‘monthly income applicable at the time of death’ will depend on the option chosen by the policyholder and the same has been defined below
    Delivers monthly income to beneficiaries in the event of the policyholder's death, with options for level or inflation-adjusted payouts
    FEATURES
    1. What it does:On death, instead of a single lump sum the nominee receives a monthly income (the chosen monthly income at inception) starting from the month after claim intimation and continuing up to the higher of 120 months or the outstanding term (months).
      You can choose Level Income or Inflation-proof Income (inflation proofing = +10% every 3 years, simple interest, capped at 200% of initial monthly income).
      • Level Income: Monthly payout remains the same throughout the payout period.
      • Inflation-proof Income: Monthly payout increases by 10% every 3 years (simple interest), capped at 200% of the initial monthly income.
        After the death of the Life Insured, there shall be no increase in the income under this variant.
      Sum Assured on death for calculation is based on monthly income × specified multiple or outstanding months (see policy).
    2. Useful when: You want to replace the insured’s salary with steady monthly payments to dependents rather than giving a single lump sum

    Common / in-built features across STPP (important highlights)
    In-built Terminal Illness benefit Terminal illness payout subject to policy terms. In the event of a terminal illness diagnosis, an accelerated payout of up to ₹1 crore is provided, depending on the plan variant
    Special Exit Value (SEV) Policyholders have the option to exit the policy from the 30th policy year onwards (excluding the last 4 policy years) and receive up to 200% of total premiums paid, depending on the policy term and premium payment term.
    Option to receive all premiums paid back,in any policy year starting 30th policyyear, but not during the last 4 policy years.
    No additional premium to be paid (free of cost).
    Cover Continuance Benefit Allows deferral of premium payments for up to 12 months after the due date, while maintaining full risk cover, provided the policy has been in force for at least 3 years with all premiums paid
    Deferral of Premium Payments: The Policyholder is allowed to defer the due premium for a period of up to 12 months from the due date, while maintaining the full risk cover under the base plan and attached riders (if any).
    This option is allowed to be exercised after completion of 3 policy years, provided all due premiums have been paid & the policy is in force
    Insta Payment on claim intimation (subject to terms)
    Accelerated Sum Assured**    		 Offers expedited claim processing with partial payouts within one working day of claim intimation, subject to submission of mandatory documents
    An accelerated benefit as applicable out of base sum assured shall be payable within 1 working day from claim registration date, provided mandatory documents are submitted.
    The subsequent payout shall be made after the claim is approved.
    Female-Centric Benefits Optional Maternity Cover & Women-specific benefits (female discount, Lifeline plus etc.) — certain female-focused benefits and discounts are available subject to additional premium/conditions
    Exclusive features for female policyholders include:
    1. Maternity Cover: Protection against certain pregnancy-related complications and congenital anomalies in newborns
    2. Lifeline Plus: Option to top-up coverage upon the death of the spouse.
    3. Premium Discount: A flat 15% discount on premiums throughout the premium payment term.
    Terminal Illness Provides a lump-sum payment in case of diagnosis of a terminal illness with a life expectancy of 12 months or less.
    et free coverage against the diagnosis of Terminal Illness and accelerate,**payout of ₹1 crore. No additional premium to be paid.

    SMART TERM ELITE PLAN (STEP)

    The Axis Max Life STEP Term Plan is a non-linked, non-participating pure risk life insurance plan designed to offer customizable protection at an affordable price. It allows policyholders to tailor their coverage based on individual needs, ensuring financial security for their loved ones in their absence.
    Axis Max Life Smart Total Elite Protection Term Plan (Non-Linked, Non-Participating Individual Pure Risk Life Insurance Plan; offers a comprehensive, customisable protection solution for you and your loved ones at an affordable price so your family can continue to step up their lifestyle even in your absence. With Axis Max Life STEP Plan, you pay only for the benefits that suit your requirement, and you have the freedom to design your own plan keeping in mind your protection needs. Since this is a term insurance plan, no maturity benefit is offered under this product.

    Features of Axis Max Life STEP

    Death Benefit
    BASE    		 Provides a guaranteed death benefit to the nominee, ensuring financial stability for your family.
    On the death of the life insured during the term of the policy, provided the policy is in-force, the insurer will pay the Guaranteed Death Benefit to the beneficiary under the Plan, which is the higher of:
    1. For Single Pay - 1.25 times the Single Premium plus underwriting extra premium if any; For Other Premium Payment Term - 10 times the Annualised Premium* plus underwriting extra premium, if any,
    2. 105% of Total Premiums paid^ plus underwriting extra premium plus loadings for modal premiums as on the date of death
    3. Base Sum Assured#:* 'Annualised Premium' shall be the premium amount payable in a year, excluding taxes, rider premiums, underwriting extra premiums and loadings for modal premiums. The annualised premium remains the same irrespective of the premium payment mode.
      ^ 'Total Premiums Paid' means total of all the premiums paid under the base product, excluding any extra premium and taxes, if collected explicitly.
      'Sum Assured on Death' means an absolute amount of benefit which is guaranteed to become payable on death of the life assured in accordance with the terms and conditions of the policy. # 'Sum Assured on Death' is the base sum assured.
      The details of benefits under this product are given below:
    4. Guaranteed Death Benefit is payable on the death of the Life Insured, provided the policy is in-force.
    5. Accelerated Benefit capped at Rs 1 crore is payable on diagnosis of Terminal Illness, provided The policy is in force.
      6.
    Terminal Illness Benefit In case of diagnosis of a terminal illness, an accelerated payout (up to ₹1 crore) is provided, and all future premiums are waived
    In case the Life Assured is diagnosed to be suffering from a disease, in the opinion of a Registered Medical Practitioner along with the insurer’s appointed doctor, which is likely to lead to their death within six months from the date of such certification, an amount capped at Rs 1 Crore is payable to the beneficiary.
    Terminal Illness benefit will accelerate the death benefit i.e. once a Terminal Illness claim is paid (payable only once during the Policy Term), the death benefit will be reduced by the terminal illness claim amount.
    Note: Only one valid Terminal Illness Benefit claim will be admissible and payable under this Policy. Post diagnosis of a terminal illness of the life insured, the policyholder shall be allowed to surrender the policy.
    All premiums due from the date of diagnosis of a terminal illness (for the base policy and options chosen) would be waived, and the policy shall continue till the death of the life insured or the end of the policy term, whichever is earlier.
    Special Exit Value A Special Exit Benefit, the total premiums paid and underwriting extra premiums paid plus loadings for modal premiums (if any), is paid if the policyholder surrenders the policy. This option can be availed in any policy year, starting 30th policy year, but not during the last 4 policy years.
    The following are the conditions for Special Exit Value:
  • The policy has to be in-force at the time of availing this value
  • This value shall not be available for policy terms less than 40 years
  • This value shall be applicable on the base cover premium only and not to additional optional benefits like Accident cover. For any optional benefits, Early Exit Value (as described below) will be payable, if applicable.
  • The policy shall be terminated after availing this value
  • This is an inbuilt product feature and no additional premium is required to be paid
    •
    Early Exit Value (EEV) Provided the policyholder has paid all due premiums, an early exit value will be applicable under the policy in case the policyholder surrenders the policy.
    The policy shall acquire an Early Exit Value subject to the criteria given below:
  • Single Pay: After payment of single premium.
  • Limited Pay: After payment of all due premiums.
  • Regular Pay: No Early Exit Value is applicable.

    • Early Exit Value = 70% of [(Total Premiums Paid plus underwriting extra premiums paid plus loading for modal premiums, if any) x (Unexpired Term/Policy Term)]
    'Early Exit Value' shall be applicable to the base cover premium and on Accident Cover option”

    Cover Continuance Benefit Allows deferral of premium payments for up to 12 months without losing coverage, useful during financial hardships
    As per this benefit, the policyholder is given the choice to defer the due premium for a period of up to 12 months from the due date, during which the full risk cover under the base plan and attached riders, if any, remains active. In the event of a claim during this period, the insurer will pay the claim as applicable after deducting the unpaid premiums, if any, as on the date of death or any other insured event covered by the base product and attached riders.
    However, this benefit can only be availed after completion of 3 policy years, provided all due premiums have been paid, and the policy is in-force.
    Note: The duration of Cover Continuance Benefit (CCB) shall be 12 consecutive policy months from the date of the first unpaid premium. The CCB shall be available multiple times with a gap of 5 policy years from the expiry date of Cover Continuance Benefit availed previously.
    Once the Cover Continuance Benefit period ends, the policyholder needs to pay the due premiums, including the premium applicable for the period of CCB, i.e. the base cover premium and additional premium (if any) e.g. rider premium and accident cover premium inclusive of underwriting extra, loading for modal premiums, and any applicable taxes.
    Cover Continuance Benefit is an inbuilt product feature, and no additional premium is required to be paid. This benefit is available to all premium paying terms (Regular, Limited & Pay Till 60) except Single pay.
    During the Cover Continuance Benefit, the policy will remain in-force with the risk cover as per terms and condition applicable under Grace Period of the policy. This is an inbuilt product feature and no additional premium is required to be paid. The policyholder needs to intimate the company 30 days (15 days in case of monthly mode) before exercising Cover Continuance Benefit. If a premium is unpaid with no prior intimation, the policy at the end of the grace period shall be treated as per the terms & conditions.
    Insta Payment on Claim Intimation Provides an immediate payout upon claim intimation to help cover urgent expenses
    As per this benefit, on receipt of intimation of death (along with required documents) after a waiting period of 1 year from the date of policy issuance or revival, an accelerated benefit as mentioned in the table out of the base sum assured, shall be payable within 1 working day from claim registration date provided all mandatory documents are submitted.
    The subsequent payout shall be made after the claim is approved.
    Note: This benefit is payable post a minimum waiting period of 1 year from the inception of the policy or revival, provided the policy is in-force.
    In case of repudiation / rejection of claim, the amount will be recovered from the nominee.

    OPTIONAL RIDERS
    Accident Cover On the death of the Life Insured due to an accident, 100% of the Accident Cover Sum Assured will be payable as a lump sum, upon approval of the claim, irrespective of the claim payout mode chosen by the nominee. This benefit shall be payable in addition to the guaranteed death benefit.
    The Accident Cover can be added to the premium-paying policy at any time during the policy term. An additional premium, on a pro-rata basis, will be charged in case the benefit is added during the middle of the policy term, and the full premium will be charged starting next policy anniversary.
    Once the Accident Cover is terminated, it cannot be added again.
    Waiver of Premium Plus Rider Waives future premiums upon diagnosis of critical illness or disability
    Critical Illness and Disability Rider Provides additional coverage upon diagnosis of specified critical illnesses or disabilities.

    WHAT IT DOES : Provides a large death benefit at low premium — protects family income, loan repayment, children’s education, etc.
    How it helps vs inflation: It protects against loss of earning capacity (i.e., protects family from the immediate financial shock). You can set the sum assured to an inflation-adjusted target
    LIMITATIONS :Term plans do not build inflation-beating savings — claim payout is fixed nominal amount (so choose cover thinking in real, inflation-adjusted terms).
    PRACTICAL TIPS:Practical tip: choose Sum Assured ≈ (current annual expenses × replacement years) × (1+inflation)^n
    for the horizon you want to secure

    Who Should Choose Which Plan?

    Choose STEP if:
  • Your only goal is maximum life cover at the lowest premium
  • You have separate investment plans like Pension Plan, FD, RD, Health Insurance Plan, SIPs, mutual funds, etc.
  • You need a straightforward term insurance solution
    • Choose STAR ULIP if:
  • You want a combination of insurance + long-term wealth creation
  • You are comfortable with market-linked returns
  • You want flexibility through multiple funds and investment strategies
    • Choose STPP if:
  • You need a term plan with more customisation
  • You prefer options like Return of Premium, Whole Life Cover, Income Protection etc
  • You want additional conveniences like Cover Continuance and Special Exit Value
    • Recommendation
  • Pure protection requirement → STEP or STPP
  • Protection + wealth accumulation → STAR ULIP
  • Need advanced term features like ROP/Whole Life/Income protection → STPP

    SAVINGS PRODUCTS (TRADITIONAL)

    A savings plan is a financial product that helps build a financial corpus for the future through regular contributions made over an extended period of time. While a majority of savings plans in India are investment focused, some of these plans can also offer additional benefits such as life insurance cover, protection of the principal invested and tax savings.
    Depending on the savings plan chosen, the wealth creation benefit received by the investor can be in the form of guaranteed returns or market-linked returns. The payouts offered by these investments can also vary ranging from a lump sum payout at maturity to a regular payouts received over a predetermined period of time.
    For example, suppose your goal is to accumulate ₹30 lakh for your child’s higher education in the next 10 years. A savings plan that provides you fixed returns of 7% p.a. can help you accumulate this amount if you invest around ₹29,500 per month for the next 10 years.

    Savings Plans in India

    Every savings plan in India has its unique benefits and limitations so no specific one can be singled out as the best savings plan in India. The choice of plan will depend on multiple factors ranging from the financial needs and risk tolerance of the investor to the liquidity requirements and expected returns. Below are some of the popular savings plans in India that suits the investment needs of various categories of investors:

    SAVING INSTRUMENTS DESCRIPTION
    RECURRING DEPOSITS
    		 A recurring deposit allows you to invest a fixed amount every month for a predetermined period.
    FEATURES
  • It promotes disciplined saving behaviour since one is required to contribute a set amount each month.
  • The interest rate is fixed at the time of account opening and is locked for the entire duration of the RD.
  • RD tenure typically ranges from 6 months to 10 years.
  • Premature redemptions are allowed subject to applicable penalty.
  • Interest earned from recurring deposits is taxable as per the applicable income tax slab rate.
    •
    FIXED DEPOSITS A fixed deposit (FD) is a traditional investment option in which you deposit a lump sum with a bank or financial institution for a specified period in exchange for a fixed rate of interest. It is usually viewed as an important part of a conservative investment strategy.
    FEATURES
  • The investment will provide guaranteed returns at an interest rate that is locked-in at the time of account opening.
  • Investors can choose from a range of tenure options, starting from a few days to several years
  • Most banks permit loan or overdraft facilities on the FD balance in case money is required before maturity.
  • Premature withdrawal is allowed with applicable penalties.
  • The interest earned on an FD is taxable according to the investor’s applicable income tax slab.
  • A special type of FD, the 5 year Tax Saver FD offers tax benefits u/s 80C if the depositor has opted for the old tax regime
    •
    MONTLY INCOME PLANS Monthly income plans are savings options designed to provide a steady stream of income at regular intervals. They are often chosen by individuals who want financial stability through periodic payouts to support everyday expenses, retirement needs, or other recurring commitments.
    FEATURES
  • A part of the invested amount or the returns is distributed at regular intervals to create a consistent income stream.
  • If the investor survives the policy term, the remaining corpus or a lump sum amount may be paid at maturity, depending on the monthly savings plan structure.
  • If the monthly income scheme includes a life insurance component and the insured passes away during the term, the nominee may receive the full sum assured regardless of the payouts already made.
  • Returns may vary depending on the performance of the underlying investments in market-linked plans.
    •
    NATIONAL PENSION SYSTEM
    (NPS)    		 The National Pension System (NPS) is a government-regulated, long-term retirement savings scheme available to employees in the public, private, and unorganised sectors. It is designed to help individuals build a retirement corpus through regular contributions.
    FEATURES
  • NPS is a market-linked retirement plan that allows investments in 4 asset classes – equity, government securities, corporate bonds and alternative investment funds.
  • NPS allows investors to flexibly to allocate funds across different asset classes.
  • Maximum age of entry in NPS is till the age of 60 years and investments can be held till the age of 75 years
  • For NPS Tier 1 account holders, tax benefits up to ₹1.5 lakh per financial year are available under Section 80C. Individuals can get an additional ₹50,000 deduction by filing their ITR under Section 80CCD(1B).
  • NPS Tier 2 account is an investment account that does not offer tax benefits in most cases. Government employees can claim tax benefit on Tier 2 contributions u/s 80C if the investments are held for at least 3 years.
  • Only 3 partial withdrawals are allowed throughout the investment period for specific reasons like marriage costs, education expenses, medical costs, etc.
    •
    KISAN VIKAS PATRA (KVP) Kisan Vikas Patra is a small savings program offered by the government to all Indian citizens. It is considered as a risk-free savings plan that doubles the investments within a given period, current 115 months (applicable till 31 March 2026).
    FEATURES
  • The scheme is supported by the Government of India and the sovereign guarantee offers stable and predictable returns.
  • This savings scheme requires a minimum investment of ₹1,000, and additional deposits can be made in multiples of ₹100. There is no maximum limit on KVP investments.
  • The scheme may be availed at any post office or authorised bank in the country.
  • Investments in KVP can be encashed prematurely after 2.5 years at specified rates from the date of investment.
    •
    PUBLIC PROVIDENT FUND
    (PPF)    		 Public Provident Fund is a long-term savings scheme that matures after 15 years from the date of account opening. Investors can contribute a minimum of ₹500 and a maximum of ₹1.5 lakh in a financial year.
    To plan your investment more effectively, you can use a PPF calculator to estimate the maturity amount based on your yearly contributions and the applicable interest rate.
    FEATURES
  • Contributions made up to ₹1.5 lakh per year qualify for tax deductions under Section 80C of the Income Tax Act, if the investor has opted for the old tax regime.
  • PPF features E-E-E (Exempt-Exempt-Exempt) tax status, meaning the contributions, the interest earned, and the maturity proceeds are all tax-exempt.
  • After initial maturity of the PPF account, multiple extensions in blocks of 5 years are allowed.
  • The account can be easily transferred between authorised banks and post offices anywhere within India
  • Loan against PPF facility is available from the 3rd to the 6th financial year.
  • Partial withdrawals against PPF account balance are permitted from the 7th year onwards.
    •
    NATIONAL SAVINGS CERTIFICATE
    (NSC)    		 National Savings Certificate (NSC) National Savings Certificate is a government-backed savings scheme that functions as a fixed-income investment option and can be opened at any post office. It is an ideal investment for investors seeking guaranteed government-backed returns and capital protection.
    FEATURES
  • The maturity period of the National Savings Certificate is 5 years.
  • Minimum deposit amount is ₹1000 and increments are allowed in multiples of ₹100.
  • There is no maximum deposit limit, however, maximum tax benefit that can be claimed in a tax year is capped at ₹1.5 lakh.
  • Investors can avail themselves of loan facilities by pledging their National Savings Certificate with the lender.
  • Investment in the NSC allows tax deductions under Section 80C for investments up to ₹1.5 lakh per financial year.
    •
    SENIOR CITIZEN SAVINGS SCHEMES
    (SCSS)    		 The Senior Citizen Savings Scheme is a government-sponsored savings scheme aimed at addressing the financial requirements of senior citizens in India. This savings plan provides a fixed income upon retirement, and an SCSS calculator can be used by the investors to project the interest earned and the maturity value.
    FEATURES
  • Individuals aged 60 years and above can open an SCSS account. Additionally, individuals aged 55 to 60 years who have opted for voluntary retirement may also be eligible.
  • Minimum deposit is ₹1,000. Maximum deposit allowed is ₹30 lakh.
  • Investment tenure is 5 years, with an option to extend for 3 more years.
  • SCSS investments (only the principal amount) qualify for tax deductions up to ₹1.5 lakh in a tax year under Section 80C if the investor has opted for the old tax regime.
  • Interest payouts from the account occur on a quarterly basis. The interest income is subject to taxation as per the individual’s tax slab.
    •
    POST OFFICE MONTHLY INCOME SCHEME
    (POMIS)    		 Post Office Monthly Income Scheme (POMIS) is a popular savings scheme offered by India Post and is considered a secure option for individuals looking for a low-risk way to save.
    FEATURES
  • There is a 1-year lock-in period, and the funds can be withdrawn prematurely.
  • Account matures after 5 years and all funds have to be withdrawn, as no extension is allowed.
  • Minimum balance required for account opening is ₹1,000. Maximum investment allowed is ₹9 lakh (Single Account) and ₹15 lakh (Joint Account).
  • A POMIS account can be opened and held by a minimum of 1 individual and a maximum of 3 adults.
  • Interest from the account balance is credited on a monthly basis. This interest, if not withdrawn does not accrue further interest.
  • Any citizen aged above 18 and residing in India can opt for this scheme. Minor aged atleast 10 years can hold the account jointly with an adult.
    •
    ATAL PENSION YOJANA (APY) Atal Pension Yojana is a government-backed retirement-focused pension scheme that is designed to provide assured pension after retirement. It was designed to address the longevity risks among unorganised sector workers by allowing them save voluntarily to secure their post-retirement finances.
    FEATURES
  • The scheme offers a guaranteed monthly pension ranging from ₹1,000 to ₹5,000, depending on the subscriber’s choice and contributions during the working years.
  • The pension is guaranteed by the Central Government, helping ensure a predictable income stream for retirees especially those working in the unorganised sector.
  • The scheme is available to Indian citizens aged 18 to 40 years who have a savings bank account.
  • Since October 2022, individuals who have filed ITR in the previous tax year are not eligible to enrol in the APY scheme.
    •
    SUKANYA SAMRIDHI YOJANA (SSY) SSY is a government-backed small savings plan that was introduced as part of the Beti Bachao, Beti Padhao program to provide financial security to the girl child. Sukanya Samriddhi Yojana gives parents or guardians a chance to save in a systematic manner towards the long-term needs for up to 2 girls.
    The maturity period for an Sukanya Samriddhi account is 21 years from the date of opening. The account can be prematurely closed if the girl child gets married after attaining 18 years of age.
    FEATURES
  • Parents or the legal guardians can open the scheme on behalf of a girl child who is below the age of 10 years.
  • The minimum deposit required for opening SSY account is ₹250, while the maximum deposit permitted in a financial year is ₹1.5 lakh
  • It provides EEE (Exempt-Exempt-Exempt) tax benefits, where contributions, interest earned, and the maturity amount are tax-exempt. However under current rules, tax benefit on contributions can be claimed only if you have opted for the old tax regime.
  • Withdrawal equal to up to 50% of the account balance is permitted to cover the account holder’s higher education expenses.
    •
    EMPLOYEE PROVIDENT FUND (EPF) The Employee Provident Fund (EPF) is a retirement savings scheme introduced by the Employees’ Provident Fund Organisation (EPFO). It allows salaried employees to contribute a portion of their income to a provident fund account, helping them build a financial corpus for retirement.
    FEATURES
  • EPF helps individuals plan for retirement and build a secure financial future through long-term savings.
  • Both the employee and employer contribute to the EPF account, helping increase the retirement corpus.
  • Generally, 12% of the employee’s basic salary is contributed, and the employer contributes a similar percentage to the EPF account.
  • EPF allows partial withdrawals for purposes such as children’s education or marriage, medical treatment, and house construction.
    •
    VOLUNTARY PROVIDENT FUND (VPF) Voluntary Provident Fund (VPF) is an extension of the EPF scheme that allows employees to contribute more than the mandatory 12% of their salary. However, an equal co-contribution by the employer is not required in this case.
    FEATURES
  • It offers the same interest rate as EPF, which is currently 8.25% p.a., subject to revisions.
  • Contributions and interest earned may be tax-free if the funds are withdrawn after a minimum investment period of five years.
  • Applicable for EEE tax benefits, so tax exemption is applicable on contribution, interest earned and . However, after Budget 2021, the exemption on the accrued interest will be applicable up to an amount of ₹2.5 lakh only
  • It is a suitable savings option for salaried individuals who wish to build a larger retirement corpus without taking market-related risks.
  • The fund allows partial withdrawals for specific purposes such as medical treatment, construction of a residential house, etc.
    •
    ENDOWMENT PLNAS Endowment plans are a combination of life insurance and savings, which are paid out as a lump sum on a maturity date or to the nominee in case the insured passes away during the policy term.
    You can choose an immediate or deferred income option, along with multiple payout options like lump-sum, yearly, half-yearly, or monthly.
    FEATURES
  • These plans offer life cover along with maturity benefits and bonuses, depending on the policy terms.
  • Returns from these savings plans are guaranteed and usually lower than those of market-linked investment options.
  • Premiums are often higher than pure term insurance policies because they include both savings and protection benefits.
  • Endowment premium payments are tax-deductible under Section 80C up to ₹1.5 lakh annual limit, if the policyholder has opted for the old tax regime. The maturity benefits are also tax-exempt under Section 10(10D), subject to applicable terms and conditions.
  • This is suitable for conservative investors who want to save for the long term to leave a legacy and also ensure the financial protection of their loved ones.
    •
    UNIT LINKED INSURANCE PLANS (ULIP) ULIPs are financial products that combine life insurance protection with investment opportunities. They are generally considered suitable for long-term financial planning, as returns depend on market performance.
    FEATURES
  • In ULIP plans, a portion of the premium is used to provide life cover, while the remaining amount is invested in market-linked instruments
  • It offers a death benefit to nominees if the insured passes away during the policy term.
  • Policyholders usually have the flexibility to choose and switch funds based on their investment strategy.
  • The maturity proceeds from ULIPs remain tax-free if the annual premium is below ₹2.5 lakh per financial year.
    •

    Differences Between Savings Plan
    & Life Insurance Plan

    There are several differences between savings plans and life insurance plans in terms of objectives, risks, tax benefits, and who these plans are ideal for. Key differences between savings plan and life insurance plan to consider when choosing between the two are as follws:

    PARAMETER SAVINGS PLAN LIFE INSURANCE PLAN
    OBJECTIVES Helps individuals build wealth through disciplined savings, with either guaranteed or market-linked returns. Provides FINANCIAL PROTECTION to nominees in the event the insured passes away during the policy term.
    RISKS Generally focuses on capital growth with relatively lower risk, although market-linked options may involve some investment risk. FOCUSES ON PROTECTING against the financial impact of the insured’s untimely demise. Term plans, for instance, provide higher cover at comparatively lower premiums.
    IDEAL FOR Individuals aiming to accumulate funds for future financial needs or long-term goals. Individuals seeking financial security for their dependents in the event of their unexpected demise.
    TAX BENEFITS Some savings plans may offer tax deductions under Section 80C (old tax regime), and certain products may provide tax-efficient returns or maturity proceeds. Premiums paid may qualify for tax deductions under Section 80C (old tax regime), and maturity proceeds may be tax-free under applicable tax provisions.

    When choosing between a savings plan and a life insurance policy, the right choice depends on your financial priorities and long-term objectives. Here is a detailed overview:

  • Choose life insurance if your main goal is to provide financial protection and income replacement for your dependants in case of an unexpected event.
  • Consider a savings plan if you want to build a fund for future goals such as children’s education, retirement, or other major expenses.
  • Life insurance plans such as endowment plans or ULIPs, may be suitable if you wish to combine both protection and savings in a single policy.
    •

    Difference Between Savings Plan
    and Investment Plan

    There are several key differences between savings plans and investment plans based on objectives, goals and suitability, liquidity, lock-in period, and other factors. Check out the details below:

    Parameters Savings Plan Investment Plans
    Objectives It is designed to preserve capital while offering gradual growth through relatively low-risk options such as FDs, PPF, or endowment policies. Its main goal is to create wealth through market-linked instruments such as equities, mutual funds, or real estate.
    Goals and Suitability Suitable for conservative investors seeking stable options for short-term or medium-term goals, such as creating an emergency fund or saving for planned expenses. Suited for long-term financial goals such as higher education planning or retirement, especially for investors willing to accept market fluctuations for potential wealth growth.
    Liquidity and Lock-in Period Many savings options have defined tenures. For example, PPF has a 15-year lock-in period, and fixed deposits may apply penalties for early withdrawals. Investments such as stocks or mutual funds generally offer higher liquidity, although some products like ELSS come with a 3-year lock-in period.
    Risk and Return Usually provide fixed or relatively stable returns with lower risk, as funds are often placed in government-backed or debt-based instruments. Returns are linked to market performance, which may provide higher gains but also involves greater volatility and risk.
    Taxation Certain savings schemes, such as PPF, SSY, or NSC, may provide tax benefits under Section 80C (old tax regime), and some may offer tax-efficient maturity proceeds depending on applicable rules. Tax implications vary depending on the investment type, such as equity or debt, and the holding period

    Benefits of Savings Plan

    1. Encourages Financial Discipline:Savings plans promote the habit of setting aside money regularly. Consistent contributions help individuals develop disciplined saving habits that support long-term financial stability.
    2. Life Cover Along With Savings : Many savings plans include a life insurance component. In case of the insured’s unfortunate demise, the family receives a payout that can provide financial support during difficult times. Using tools such as a life insurance calculator can help you estimate the level of coverage needed to adequately protect your family.
    3. Helps Achieve Financial Goals : You can use a savings plan to slowly build a corpus towards significant life objectives. They can involve buying a car, going on a vacation, or financing your child’s education or your retirement.
    4. Flexible Investment Options :Most savings plans offer flexibility in terms of allowing you to choose how to invest your funds based on your risk preference. For example, ULIPs allow you to switch between funds based on the current market conditions.
    5. Tax Advantages :As most of the savings schemes cover life insurance benefits, they can entail tax deductions on Section 80C of the Income Tax Act (old tax regime). Individuals may claim deductions of up to ₹1,50,000 per year on eligible contributions, subject to applicable tax rules.
    6. Potential or Guaranteed Returns :Depending on the type of savings plan selected, you may receive guaranteed benefits or market-linked returns at maturity. Some plans also offer the option to receive payouts at regular intervals while the policy remains active.

    SWAG PAR and SWAG NON-PAR are both long-term savings-cum-insurance products, but they belong to different categories of traditional life insurance plans

    The Axis Max Life Smart Wealth Advantage Guarantee (SWAG) Plan is a comprehensive financial solution designed to cater to the sophisticated needs. It seamlessly integrates guaranteed returns with lifelong protection, facilitating effective legacy planning.
    The Smart Wealth Advantage Guarantee (SWAG) Plan offers a suite of five distinct variants, each tailored to meet specific financial goals and life stages.

    >

    1. SWAG PAR (Smart Wealth Advantage Guaranteed – Participating Plan)

    A Participating (PAR) plan allows policyholders to participate in the insurer's profits through bonuses declared from time to time. The maturity benefit generally consists of:

  • Guaranteed Benefits
  • Reversionary / Cash Bonuses (if declared)
  • Terminal Bonus (if applicable)
  • Life Insurance Cover

    • Since bonuses depend on the insurer's performance, a portion of the returns is non-guaranteed. Therefore, actual maturity benefits may vary.
    Key Characteristics

  • Insurance + Savings
  • Profit-sharing through bonuses
  • Potentially higher long-term returns than Non-Par plans
  • Part of maturity value is not guaranteed
  • Suitable for investors comfortable with some uncertainty in returns
    •

    2. SWAG NON-PAR (Smart Wealth Advantage Guaranteed – Non-Participating Plan)
    A Non-Participating (NON-PAR) plan does not share insurer profits with policyholders.
    The benefits are defined at inception and generally include:

  • Guaranteed Maturity Benefit
  • Guaranteed Income (if chosen)
  • Guaranteed Death Benefit

    • No bonuses or dividends are payable. The insurer bears the investment risk and the policyholder receives pre-defined benefits.

  • Insurance + Guaranteed Savings
  • Entire benefit structure known upfront
  • No dependence on insurer profits
  • Predictable cash flows
  • Suitable for conservative investors seeking certainty
    •

    Bonuses Available (not guaranteed) Not Available
    Guaranteed Returns Partial Mostly/Entirely Guaranteed
    Return Potential Higher but uncertain Lower but predictable
    Risk Leve Moderate Low

This plan is tailored to provide a blend of guaranteed lifelong income, protection, and wealth accumulation, catering to individuals seeking financial security and legacy planning.

    Key Features of SMART WIBE
    Policy Continuance Benefit In the event of the policyholder's demise, the policy continues without the need for future premium payments, ensuring that the nominee receives all due benefits.
    Multiple Variants: Options like Early Income, Early Income with Guaranteed Money Back, and Deferred Income allow customization based on financial goals.
    Deferment of Survival Benefits Policyholders can choose to accrue survival benefits and withdraw them as needed, earning interest over the accrued benefits.
    Enhanced Liquidity Certain variants provide survival benefits starting from the 2nd policy year, offering early liquidity.
    Choice of Income Period Flexibility to choose the income period, including options up to 100 years of age
    Optional Riders Add-ons like waiver of premium, accidental death & dismemberment, term plus, and critical illness riders enhance the policy's coverage
    Guaranteed Lifelong Income Receive a steady, guaranteed income stream until the age of 100, ensuring financial stability throughout your lifetime
    Return of Premiums Benefit from a 50% return of total premiums paid at age 85 and a 100% return at age 100, effectively providing a 150% return on premiums over the policy term
    Enhanced Protection Includes an in-built accidental death benefit, offering an additional layer of financial security to your loved ones
    Flexible Premium Payment Terms Choose from various premium payment durations to align with your financial planning and convenience.
    Liquidity Options Accrue your income and withdraw it at any time during the policy term, providing flexibility to meet unforeseen financial needs.
    Tax Benefits Premiums paid and benefits received may be eligible for tax deductions and exemptions under prevailing tax laws

    SAVINGS ADVANTAGE PLAN (SAP)

    All of us need a sound financial plan that can provide support to our family if an unexpected event were to happen. Life Insurance is a key element of any good financial plan.
    Also, in your life, you have short term goals and goals that are relatively longer in duration. For any kind of life stage need that you may have such as buying a car, planning for child’s education/marriage, building corpus for your/spouse’s retirement, etc., you need a financial instrument where you can systematically save for fulfilling all your life stage needs. What if your life insurance plan provides you a corpus at your desired milestone to meet your goals while providing risk coverage against exigencies?
    Presenting Axis Max Life Savings Advantage Plan that will help you grow your systematic savings and build a corpus to address all your life stage needs while providing for risk coverage at the same time to take care of your loved ones in case of an exigency.

    ABOUT THE PRODUCT

    AXIS MAX LIFE SAVINGS ADVANTAGE PLAN is a Non-Linked Participating Individual Life Insurance Savings plan that offers

  • Risk Coverage throughout the Policy Term i.e.
    • a sum of Guaranteed Death Benefit, accrued Guaranteed Additions along with accrued Paid Up Additions (if any) and Terminal Bonus (if any) on Death of life insured on or before completion of 10 policy years
    • a sum of 110% of Guaranteed Death Benefit along with accrued Guaranteed Additions, accrued Paid Up Additions (if any) & Terminal Bonus (if any) in case of death of the life insured after 10 policy years
  • a sum of 110% of Guaranteed Sum Assured on Maturity along with accrued Guaranteed Additions, accrued Paid Up Additions (if any) and Terminal Bonus (if any) on Maturity
  • an option to convert the lumpsum Maturity/Death Benefit in equal monthly or annual installments for 10 years. At any time during the payout, you/nominee, as the case may be, can choose to commute the future incomes into lumpsum
    •

    KEY FEATURES & BENEFITS SAVINGS ADVANTAGE PLAN

    This product offers you:

    1. Choice of Premium Payment Terms and Policy Terms: You have the flexibility to choose from various premium payment terms & policy terms as per your requirement. Thus, this feature enables you to decide the period for which you wish to save and the time when you need monies to fulfil your particular life stage need.
    2. Guaranteed Additions: This plan provides you guaranteed 5.5% of Guaranteed Sum Assured on Maturity as Guaranteed Additions at the end of each year for first five policy years to boost your benefits
    3. Death Benefit: Death Benefit In case of death of the life insured on or before completion of 10 policy years, Guaranteed Death Benefit along with accrued Guaranteed Additions, Paid Up Additions (if any) & Terminal Bonus (if any) shall be payable.
      In case of death of the life insured after 10 policy years, 110% of Guaranteed Death Benefit along with accrued Guaranteed Additions, Paid Up Additions (if any) & Terminal Bonus (if any) shall be payable.
    4. Maturity Benefit : You enjoy 110% of Guaranteed Sum Assured on Maturity along with accrued Guaranteed Additions, accrued Paid Up Additions (if any) and Terminal Bonus (if any).
    5. Settlement and Commutation Benefit : You/nominee, as the case may be, have the flexibility to convert the lumpsum maturity benefit/death benefit into regular income for 10 years basis your requirement
    6. Tax Benefit: You may be entitled to tax benefits on the premiums paid and benefits received by you as per the prevailing tax laws.

    ANNUAL BONUS The bonus shall be declared in the form of Paid Up Additions every year post completion of 2 Policy Years. .
    Paid Up Additions shall be payable on earlier of surrender, death or maturity. However, in case of surrender, only surrender value of accrued Paid Up Additions (if any) shall be payable. .
    Following bonus utilization options shall be available to You at the Proposal Form stage:
    1. Paid Up Additions: The bonus once declared shall accrue and be payable in full on earlier of death or maturity. In case of surrender of policy, the surrender value of all accrued Paid Up Additions shall be payable to You.
      Paid Up Additions shall participate in future bonuses and You shall have the flexibility to partially/fully surrender the Paid Up Additions at any time during the Policy Term in which case the surrender value of the surrendered Paid Up Additions shall be payable. The minimum surrender value of surrendered Paid Up Additions shall not be less than ₹5,000.
      Please note that this option will not be allowed in case the Policy is in Reduce Paid-up mode.
    2. Premium Offset: Upon declaration of Paid Up Additions each year, the surrender value of Paid Up Additions shall be utilized to offset the future premium. In the event where the surrender value of Paid Up Additions exceeds the Premium payable by You to Us under this Policy, We shall pay such balance to You.
      However, if the surrender value of Paid Up Additions is not sufficient to offset the Premium payable by You to Us under this Policy, then, You shall pay the balance Premium to Us.
      After completion of the Premium Payment Term, surrender value of Paid Up Additions shall be payable to You every year till the end of Policy Term.
      There is no minimum limit for utilizing Paid Up Additions to offset future premiums.
    3. Paid In Cash: Upon declaration of Paid Up Additions each year, the surrender value of Paid Up Additions shall be payable to You every year till the end of Policy Term
    The surrender value of the Paid Up Additions will be determined basis the surrender value factor for Paid Up Additions. Please note that these rates are fixed, but may be revised by Us basis the actual experience of the company, subject to prior approval from the IRDAI.
    You can change the bonus option anytime during the Policy Term by giving Us a written request, which shall than be effective from the subsequent Policy Anniversary.
    The bonus option will automatically change to Paid Up Additions, if not already the case, in case of assignment of the Policy.
    TERMINAL BONUS Terminal Bonus is an additional bonus paid only ONCE, on the earlier of death, surrender or maturity, provided the policy has been in force for at least five years i.e. payable in case of claims made from end of 60th month onwards. However, in case of Surrender, only the Surrender Value of the Terminal Bonus shall be payable
    MATURITY BENEFIT
    Payable on Maturity of the policy provided
    the policy is in-force    		 In case the life insured has survived till the end of the policy term, the following shall be payable on maturity:
    SUM OF:
    1. 110% of Guaranteed Sum Assured on Maturity
    2. Accrued Guaranteed Additions
    3. Accrued Paid Up Additions, if any
    4. Terminal Bonus, if any
    Sum Assured on Maturity means an absolute amount of benefit
    which is guaranteed to become payable at the end of the policy term
    i.e. on maturity of the policy in accordance with the terms & conditions of the policy.
    Settlement and Commutation OptionYou have following two settlement options available to receive the ‘Maturity Benefit’:
    1. Lump Sum Benefit: You can choose to take the entire ‘Maturity Benefit’ as lump sum payout.
    2. Regular Monthly/Annual Income for 10 years: You can choose to take the ‘Maturity Benefit’ as monthly income payable over 120 months or annual income payable over 10 years.
    The terms of the settlement option shall vary depending upon the prevailing investment conditions at the time of settlement. The then interest rate at which the settlement option shall be valued will be based on the 5-year G-Sec yield, prevailing at that time
    DEATH BENEFIT
    Payable on the death of the Life Insured    		 For Single Pay variant
    A SUM OF THE FOLLOWING:
    1. Guaranteed Death Benefit
    2. Accrued Guaranteed Addition
    3. Accrued Paid Up Additions (if any)
    4. Terminal Bonus (if any)
    Where Guaranteed Death benefit
  • 125% of the Single Premium
  • Guaranteed Sum Assured on Maturity
  • Any absolute amount assured to be paid on death
    (which is 110% of Guaranteed Sum Assured on Maturity)
    •  For Limited Pay and Regular Pay variant
    Death of Life Insured before or on completion of 10 policy years
    A SUM OF THE FOLLOWING:
    1. Guaranteed Death Benefit
    2. Accrued Guaranteed Additions
    3. Accrued Paid Up Additions (if any)
    4. Terminal Bonus (if any)
    Death of Life Insured after completion of 10 policy years
    A SUM OF THE FOLLOWING:
    1. 110% x Guaranteed Death Benefit
    2. Accrued Guaranteed Additions
    3. Accrued Paid Up Additions (if any)
    4. Terminal Bonus (if any)
    where the Guaranteed Death Benefit for Limited Pay and Regular Pay variant is defined as the higher of:
  • 11 times the (Annualised Premium plus underwriting extra premium, if any)
  • 105% of ( total premiums paid plus underwriting extra premium
    plus loading for modal premiums as on the date of death
    of Life Insured)
  • Guaranteed Sum Assured on Maturit
  • Any absolute amount assured to be paid on death
    (which is 110% of Guaranteed Sum Assured on Maturity)
    •
    1. Annualised Premium shall be the premium amount payable in a Policy Year, excluding the
      Underwriting Extra Premium,
      loadings for modal premium,
      Rider Premiums and applicable taxes, cesses or levies
    2. Total Premiums Paid means the total of all the premiums paid under the base plan, excluding any extra premium and taxes, if collected explicitly.
    3. Underwriting Extra Premium means an additional amount charged by Us, as per Underwriting Policy, which is determined based on disclosures made by the Policyholder in the Proposal Form or any other information received by Us, including the medical examination report of the Life Insured.
    Settlement and Commutation OptionThe Settlement Option can be exercised by you/nominee only at the time of receiving the ‘Death Benefit’ under this plan.
    You/nominee have following two settlement options available to receive the ‘Death Benefit’:
    1. Lump Sum Benefit: You/nominee can choose to take the entire ‘Death Benefit’ as a lump sum payout.
    2. Regular Monthly/Annual Income for 10 years: You/nominee can choose to take 12.46% of ‘Death Benefit’ as annual income payable for 10 years, or 1.07% of ‘Death Benefit’ as monthly income payable for 120 months. The income will be payable from the monthly policy anniversary following the date of death of Life Insured.
    At any time during the income phase, You/nominee shall have the right to commute the remaining payouts by submitting a written request to Us. On receipt of such a request, We shall pay the present value of all future payouts discounted at the rate of 5.25% p.a. to You/nominee.
    TERMINAL ILLNESS
    Life Insured suffering from Terminal Illness    		 While this Policy is in force (including RPU mode), should the Life Insured be diagnosed to be suffering from a disease which,
    in the opinion of a Medical Practitioner and the concurrence of the Company’s appointed doctor, is likely to lead to the death of the Life Insured within six months
    from the date of such certification from the Medical Practitioner, the Company shall, at your request, pay the Benefits to the Life Insured under this policy as follows:
    Up to 50% of the Guaranteed Maturity Sum Assured at the date of intimation
    (or RPU Sum Assured, if applicable), subject to a maximum cumulative amount of 10 lakhs under all policies
    which provide for The Terminal Illness Benefit, then in force with the Company, on the approval of Terminal Illness claim filed; and upon the payment of Terminal Illness Benefit(s), the benefits under all policies then in force with the Company with respect to the Life Insured, which provides for this Terminal Illness Benefit will be proportionately reduced and will be payable in accordance with the terms of the respective policies.
    The Terminal Illness Benefit paid will be offset from the policy proceeds at the time of termination of the policy (Death, Surrender or Maturity). The terminal illness benefit can be availed of only once during the policy term. During the period of survival of the Life Insured, all premiums due shall be paid to Keep this policy in force, and the bonuses will be paid on the original Guaranteed Sum Assured on Maturity.
    RIDERS The product offers following 3 riders
    1. Axis Max Life Term Plus Rider: This rider provides additional risk coverage in case of death of life insured
    2. Axis Max Life Accidental Death & Dismemberment Rider:This rider provides additional benefit in case of death of the life insured or dismemberment of the life insured caused by accident.
    3. Axis Max Life Waiver Of Premium Plus Rider: This rider provides waiver for all future premiums under a policy on the earlier happening of either of the following events, provided the policy is in force:
      • Critical Illness; or
      • Dismemberment; or
      • Death (only when Life Insured and Policyholder are different individuals)
    4. Axis Max Life Critical Illness and Disability Rider : This rider provides additional lump sum benefit in case of critical illness diagnosis
    5. The above riders and their subsequent versions may be attached to this product or any future versions of this product
    6. There is no overlap in the benefits offered under different riders & base products, and benefits wherever applicable, shall be payable in addition to the base benefit
    7. A rider, if any, will not be offered if the term of the rider exceeds the outstanding term under the base policy.
