    ULIP PRODUCTS

    Objectives

    Axis Max Life’s ULIP products are designed to combine life insurance protection with market-linked investment opportunities. The goal is to help policyholders:

    1. Grow their wealth over the long term
    2. Protect their family’s financial future in case of unforeseen events
    3. Achieve life goals like retirement planning, children’s education, or wealth accumulation

    ULIP-AN INTRO

    A Unit-Linked Insurance Plan (ULIP) is a financial product that combines the benefits of life insurance cover and investment in one plan. When a policyholder buys a ULIP, portion of the premium paid goes towards securing the life insurance plan and the remainder is invested.
    ULIPs offer a high degree of flexibility allowing policyholders to invest in various kinds of funds based on risk appetite. ULIP investment are subject to a lock-in period of five years and tax benefits under section 80C of the Income Tax Act under the old tax regime, as per current tax rules.
    Because ULIP returns are not guaranteed and contingent upon market performance, ULIPs are best suited as a long-term investment option. Be it for creating wealth or a retirement plan, ULIPs fit into the needs of various types of investors. Additionally, as per current tax rules,
    ULIP returns are tax-free in the hands of the investor as per details specified u/s 10(10D) of the Income Tax Act, 1961. However, the charges, such as premium allocation and fund management fees, need to be considered before purchasing a ULIP plan.
    It should be note that the risks in the investment portfolio of a ULIP are borne by the policyholder.
    In other words, investing in one of the best ULIPs provides a flexible approach to investment planning. ULIPs help you safely balance your fund with equity and debt components, with options to switch as the market changes. At the same time, a Unit linked insurance plan protects your investments and life goals while offering financial coverage.

    Key Features of ULIPs

    ULIP are unique type of life insurance that offers wealth creation benefits. Mentioned below are some key features that set ULIPs apart from other life insurance offerings in India:

    1. Investment and Insurance Benefits Under a Single Plan: The primary purpose of the best unit linked insurance plan or ULIP is to help you avail of maximal wealth appreciation on your ULIP investment through different market-linked instruments and returns. At the same time, the ULIP provides comprehensive life insurance coverage benefits to you and your loved ones throughout the policy tenure.
    2. Switch between different Fund Options: You can switch between the available equity and debt fund options under your unit linked insurance plan or ULIP at any time during the Policy Term. You can make up to a fixed number of switches within a financial year without incurring any additional charges. To know whether your chosen ULIP plan offers free switches, please refer to the policy document.
    3. Premium Redirection: When you invest in the best ULIP, you may redirect your future premiums between different available funds options at any time. You would have to quote your Policy Number and specify the fund(s) to which you want to redirect the premium. You may also specify the percentage of premium you wish to allocate to each fund.
    4. Partial WithdrawalsAll ULIPs have an initial lock-in period of 5 years. You can make a fixed number of partial withdrawals from the accumulated fund value without incurring any additional charges after the completion of the lock-in period.
    5. Dual Benefits: ULIPs provide both protection and wealth creation in a single plan. A portion of your premium goes towards life insurance cover, while the rest is invested in market-linked funds. This dual structure offers financial security along with a maturity corpus for long-term goals.
    6. Choice of Funds and Flexibility to Switch: ULIP offers a wide range of fund options, which are based on your risk appetite and goals. Some of the fund options are: Equity funds, Debt funds, and Balanced/Hybrid funds. Another major feature of ULIP is the freedom to switch between funds. You can switch multiple times within a year. Many ULIPs offer the benefit of unlimited free fund switches
    7. 5 Year Lock-In Period: All ULIPs have a mandatory lock-in period of 5 years. During this period, you cannot surrender your policy or make partial withdrawals, except in case of death. After 5 years, partial withdrawals are usually allowed, subject to conditions. The lock-in promotes long-term discipline and helps your investments benefit from the power of compounding.
    8. Transparent Charges: The charges in ULIPs are disclosed upfront at the time of policy purchase. Common charges include:
      • Premium Allocation Charge
      • Mortality Charge
      • Fund Management Charge
      • Policy Administration Charge
        • There is a cap on the overall charges, which is aimed at protecting policyholders
    9. Death and Maturity Benefits: ULIP offers both death and maturity benefits. Here is closer look at how the maturity and life cover benefits if a unit linked insurance plan work
    10. Death Benefit: Nominees typically receive the higher of the sum assured or the accumulated fund value.
    11. Maturity Benefit: If you survive the policy term, you receive the fund value

    How does a ULIP Plans Work?

    Under a unit linked insurance plan (ULIP), the investment risk in the portfolio is borne by you (as a policyholder.) The primary purpose of buying the best ULIP is to secure your loved ones financially against any unforeseen events.

    1. Premium Payment: : The policyholder pays a regular premium to the insurance company either monthly, quarterly, half-yearly, or annually
      When you invest in the best ULIP, a portion of your premium is allocated for the life insurance cover as insurance.
    2. Life Cover and Investment: A portion of the premium is dedicated to life insurance coverage, while the rest of the premium is invested in various securities, such as debt, equity, or balanced funds, depending on the investor’s risk appetite and preferences.The rest is invested in various equity and debt fund options, as part of the investment.
    3. Your money is invested in the market-linked funds that you choose.
    4. Units Allocation: : The insurance company allocates units to the investor based on the invested amount, measured by Net Asset Value (NAV), which fluctuates with asset performance. The total corpus invested is divided into ‘units’ with a specific face value, and you are allocated "Units" in proportion to the amount you invest.
    5. At any point in time, the value of each unit is referred to as the Net Asset Value (or NAV).
    6. The NAV reflects any increase or decrease in the value of the underlying assets.
    7. If you make partial withdrawals from the accumulated corpus, the corresponding number of Units is sold.
    8. Similarly, the ULIP policy charges are deducted in the form of units.
    9. Maturity Benefits : The investor will receive the fund value at maturity based on the total units allocated to them and the fund's current NAV. At the time of maturity, you have the option to receive the total value of the fund, either as a lump sum, or monthly instalments paid over a specific period, as per the terms and conditions of the ULIP plan.
    10. Fund Management: : Fund managers track and manage the investment
    11. Death Benefits: In the event of the policyholder's sudden demise, the nominee receives the sum assured or the fund value, whichever is higher.In case of your demise within the policy tenure, the death benefit payable to your family will be the higher of the:
    12. Sum Assured or Total Fund Value (as on the day of death)
    13. Sum Assured plus Total Fund Value
      14.

    How Is ULIP Plan Structured?

    The investment options under ULIP plan or Unit Linked Insurance Plan are structured similar to those of mutual funds.
    ULIP plans pool investments from different investors before they are allocated to different fund options based on individual preferences.
    The assets under ULIP plans are managed by dedicated fund managers, whose focus is towards accomplishing specified investment objectives. As an investor, you can buy shares or 'units' in a single strategy or choose to diversify your investments across several market-linked ULIP funds
    When you choose to buy into a ULIP fund, you must first commit an initial lump sum payment. Subsequently, you have to make premium payments towards the plan – annual, semi-annual, or monthly. The premium payment obligation varies from one ULIP plan to another, as evident through the estimates made through the ULIP calculator. The premium invested in a ULIP plan is proportionally invested towards a specified investment mandate.
    However, ULIP means flexibility to investors, allowing them to choose to adjust their fund preferences, depending upon their needs, throughout the investment duration

    How to Calculate ULIP Returns and Premiums

    You can calculate ULIP returns based on absolute returns and CAGR. Here are the formulae to do so:

    1. ABSOLUTE RETURNS: Using absolute returns provides you with the percentage growth in your investment value after deducting the ULIP charges. This does not consider the time period over which this growth has occured. The formula to calculate absolute returns is this
      Absolute returns = [ (Current value - Value at the time of purchase) / Value at the time of purchase ] x 100
    2. COMPOUND ANNUAL GROWTH RATE (CAGR): Using CAGR, you can calculate the compounded annual growth rate that your investment has achieved over a specific time period. The formula is as follows:
      CAGR = { [ (Current value / Value at the time of purchase) ^ (1/ number of years) ] - 1 } x 100

    NAV & UNITS in ULIP

    UNITS & NAVs : In ULIP plans, your investment works like mutual funds through units and NAV. The number of units you hold represents your ownership in the fund. NAV is the price per unit, which is calculated daily.

    \[ NAV = \frac{Market Value of Investments+Assets-Liabilities} {Total Number of Units} \]

    NET ASSET VALUE (NAV) :The investment part buys units of the selected fund. The price of one unit is called the NAV.
    • Mutual funds → units + NAV
    • ULIPs → also units + NAV
      • The difference is that ULIPs combine insurance + investment.
    NAV changes daily because the underlying investments move with the market.If the fund invests mostly in equities: The standard formula is: NAV = ("Market Value of Investments" + "Assets" - "Liabilities") / "Total Number of Units"
    • Market up → NAV rises
    • Market down → NAV falls
      • Axis Max Life states that ULIP NAV is calculated daily based on market value of assets and liabilities.

    PREMIUM MECHANISM IN ULIP

    PREMIUM ALLOCATION : ULIP premium is split into two portions after deduction of any applicable fees and charges.
    The first thing that you need to understand is ULIP premium. You can pay the ULIP premium MONTHLY, QUARTERLY ot ANNUALLY.
    After deducting applicable charges, part of the premium is paid for LIFE INSURANCE COVER, and the remaining amount is allocated to the chosen market-linked funds.
    This ensures both protection and wealth creation in a single plan.
    MECHANISM OF PREMIUM IN ULIP:In an Axis Max Life ULIP, there is no fixed percentage split such as "30% for insurance and 70% for investment." The actual allocation is variable and depends on the specific ULIP product, your age, premium amount, policy year, sum assured, and applicable charges.
    HOW A PREMIUM ACTUALLY DISBORSED: Suppose you pay a premium of ₹1,00,000: Premium Allocation Charge (if applicable) is deducted first.
    The balance is invested into the selected fund(s).
    Every month, Mortality Charges (cost of life insurance cover) and Policy Administration Charges are deducted by cancelling units from the fund account.
    Fund Management Charges (FMC) are adjusted through the NAV of the fund.
    Therefore:
    Investment Component = Premium − Charges
    Insurance Component = Mortality Charges deducted for risk cover The ratio changes every year and is not predetermine
    It is variable. For example, a healthy 30-year-old may pay very low mortality charges initially, so over 95% of the premium (after allocation charges) may effectively go toward investment.
    As age increases, mortality charges generally increase, causing a larger portion of the premium/fund value to be used for life cover.
    Many investors assume charges are deducted only from the investment side, but a ULIP has multiple charges:
    Thus, even the cost of life insurance (mortality charge) is deducted from the investment fund by cancelling units every month

  • One portion is used to provide life insurance cover benefit, including risk cover. This provides a sum assured to your nominees in case of your demise within the policy period.
  • The remaining portion is allocated towards one or more funds of your choice. This portion is ultimately invested in various market-linked instruments such as equity stocks, corporate bonds, government securities, etc.
    •

    Types of ULIP Plans Available in India

    Currently available ULIPs in India are typically clasified based on the specific life goals they are designed to achieve. Different types of ULIP plans in India include the following:

    1. PENSION ULIP: A pension or Retirement ULIP focuses on building a retirement corpus. At maturity, you can take a lump sum or use a part of it to buy an annuity plan for regular income. Such plans also allow fund switches, enabling you to modify your investments based on market conditions or life stages.
    2. EDUCATION ULIP: Education or Children ULIPs are designed for a child’s future needs, like education or marriage. They offer add-on benefits such as waiver of future premiums in the case of demise of the parent/guardian during the policy term.
    3. WEALTH CREATION ULIP: This type of ULIP focuses on long-term capital appreciation for goals like buying a house, wealth building, or legacy planning. Such plans can be an ideal choice if you are in your 20s or 30s and wish to generate capital in the long run.
    4. PROTECTION ORIENTED ULIPs: Health- or Protection-Oriented ULIPs might include certain riders for critical illness or enhanced health benefits. Although such plans do not replace a comprehensive health insurance policy, they can provide an additional financial cushion in case you are diagnosed with a critical illness.

    Types of Charges in ULIP?

    Let us take a closer look at the different ULIP charges offered by Axis Max Life Insurance:

    1. Premium Allocation Charge:The Premium Allocation Charge is expressed as a percentage of the premium received and is levied against the allocation of variable premium amounts against different fund options.
    2. Fund Management Charge: This is a charge levied as a percentage of the value of assets and shall be appropriated, usually daily, by adjusting the Net Asset Value (NAV) of the Fund. The rate to be levied will be equal to the annual rate, as given above, divided by 365 and multiplied by the number of days that have elapsed since the previous unit valuation date.
    3. Policy Administration Charge: This is a charge expressed as a percentage of premiums paid for all variants and is levied at each monthly anniversary by cancelling proportionate units starting from the date of commencement of the policy
    4. Mortality Charges: Mortality charge is levied for providing risk cover to the Life Insured during the Policy Term. This charge is unisex and is levied on the attained age of the Life Insured on the Sum at Risk, and these charges are guaranteed for the entire Policy Term.
    5. Surrender / Discontinuance Charge: This charge shall be levied on the Fund Value at the time of Discontinuance of Policy or effecting Complete Withdrawal (Surrender), whichever is earlier.
    6. Switch Charge: A maximum of twelve Switches are allowed in any policy year and are free of charge. Switches may be permitted during the settlement period.
    7. Premium Redirection Charge:A maximum of six Premium Redirections are allowed in each policy year and are free of any charge.
    8. Partial Withdrawal: After the first five policy years, a maximum of two partial withdrawals are allowed in a policy year and are free of any charge. No partial withdrawal will be permitted during the period of discontinuance and settlement period.

    ULIP vs OTHER INVESTMENT OPTIONS

    Knowing how ULIPs stack up against other popular investing options can help you make better financial decisions. The table below shows the key similarities and differences between ULIPs and other common investment options:

    Investment Option WHAT'S COMMON
    with ULIP    		 HOW THEY DIFFER
    MUTUAL FUNDS
  • Both are market-linked and managed by professional fund experts.
  • Offer multiple fund categories, such as equity, debt, or hybrid options.
    •
  • ULIPs include life insurance protection; mutual funds do not.
  • ULIPs have a mandatory 5-year lock-in period, while most mutual funds allow easier withdrawals (except for ELSS).
  • Both offer tax benefits, but for ULIPs, it’s under Section 80C (under old tax regime); only ELSS funds qualify under the same.
  • Mutual funds usually come with lower fund management charges.
    •
    Traditional Life Insurance
  • Both provide a life cover component.
  • Helpful in building long-term financial stability.
    •
  • ULIPs offer market-driven returns, while traditional policies provide fixed, guaranteed returns.
  • ULIPs allow flexible switching between funds, whereas traditional plans do not.
  • ULIPs are more transparent in terms of charges and fund performance.
    •
    Public Provident Fund (PPF)
  • Both qualify for tax deductions under Section 80C.
  • Encourage disciplined, long-term savings.
    •
  • PPF offers government-guaranteed fixed returns, whereas ULIPs are subject to market fluctuations.
  • PPF has a 15-year tenure, while ULIPs offer multiple policy term options.
  • ULIPs include life cover; PPF does not
  • PPF has an annual deposit cap of ₹1.5 lakh, whereas ULIPs have no such limit.
    •
    National Pension System (NPS)
  • Both are market-linked and provide tax-saving benefits.
  • Designed for long-term wealth creation.
    •
  • NPS is primarily focused on retirement planning; ULIPs can serve various financial goals
  • ULIPs offer life insurance coverage, while NPS does not.
  • NPS generally has lower charges but fewer fund-switching options compared to ULIPs.
    •
    Fixed Deposits (FDs)
  • Both can be used for long-term savings and wealth accumulation.
    •
  • FDs offer fixed, guaranteed returns; ULIPs provide market-based potential for higher gains.
  • ULIPs include life insurance coverage; FDs don’t.
  • ULIPs are more tax-efficient on maturity, while FDs offer higher liquidity and easier withdrawals
    •

    Unit Linked Insurance Plans (ULIPs) combine the benefits of life insurance cover and market-linked investments within a single policy. One part of the premium paid for the policy is paid for life insurance cover, while the remaining portion is set aside for market-linked investments. Such investment instruments can be equity, debt, or hybrid funds.
    A ULIP is a dual benefit insurance plan that combines the protetcion of life insurance with long-term wealth creation through market-linked investments.
    A portion of your premium is used to provide life cover, and the remaining amount is invested in MARKET-LINKED ASSETS. Unlike Traditional insurance plans, ULIPs provide you with the flexibility to invest in EQUITY, DEBT, or HYBRID FUNDS based on your financial goals.
    ULIP plans may suit individuals with moderate-to-high risk appetite looking for long-term wealth creation and tax-efficient investment options.

    FUND OPTIONS : ULIP fund options are categorised by risks, which can be summed up as follows:

  • EQUITY FUNDS : These funds primarily invest in equity-oriented instruments. These are prone tohigh level of risk, however capable of providing inflation-beating returns in the long-term.
  • DEBT FUNDS: Invest mainly in fixed-income securities such as government or corporate bonds.These investments are typically less volatile than equities, however returns tend to be relatively
    •

    4. MATURITY BENEFITS : Maturity benefit is payable on survival till the end of the policy term. It is equal to the “Fund Value”on the maturity date. The insurer pays the maturity benefit in the form of a lump sum, which is credited directly to your bank account

    Before investing in a ULIP, you need to understand what is ULIP and how it works. You need tounderstand its features like protection, charges, risks, and market-linked return potential. ULIPs work in a few steps, and every investor needs to understand them clearly.

    1. FUND ALLOCATION: ULIP premium is invested in equity, debt, and hybrid funds based on the investor’s financial goals,and risk appetite. EQUITY FUNDS involve high risks but offer high returns too. On the other hand, DEBT FUNDS are low risk but offer stable returns. Hybrid funds are a mixture of debt and equity, ensuringmoderate risk.
    2. ULIP FUND NAV: The growth of your investment depends on the NAV (Net Asset Value) of the ULIP fund that youhave selected, which reflects its per-unit market value. NAV is subject to daily fluctuations based on
    3. INSURANCE COVER: A part of your ULIP premium is allocated for life insurance, which ensures that your nominee will receive a lump sum payout in case of your demise. The sum assured helps cover your family's expenses, your child's education, debts, and maintenance of their lifestyle, even in your absence.Thus, a ULIP ensures both financial security and long-term growth.
    4. FLEXIBILTY OF INVESTMENT : ULIPs empower you to adapt to changing needs by switching between equity, debt, or balanced funds, or opting for partial withdrawals after a ulip lock-in period . This lets you realign with goals like retirement or a child's education without exiting entirely
    5. CHARGES: ULIP includes deductions for fund management fees, premium allocation expenses, mortalitycharges, etc. Such charges can reduce your overall returns. So, when purchasing a ULIP plan, reviewthe policy documents carefully to know what is ULIP plan, along with various applicable charges toavoid them.
    6. RETURNS: Returns from your ULIP fund depend on your fund choice and market conditions. Equity funds offerhuge returns, but they are subject to market volatility. However, debt funds ensure stable returnswith less volatility. Holding your funds for the long term helps maximise wealth through compounding.

      7. Fund Option Under ULIPs

      Some of the most common investment options available under ULIP plans are

      1. EQUITY FUNDS: In an equity fund of ULIP plans, the allocated investment amount is used to purchase STOCKS, which have a Net Asset Value (or NAV) associated with them., NAV is the price per share (or 'unit') in a Fund.
        As the ULIP full form suggests, ULIP plan is a market-linked instrument, so the investments in equity carry high inherent risk because of market fluctuations. However, equity investments can also be the most rewarding.
      2. DEBT FUNDS: The premium allocated towards debt funds is used to invest in instruments such as Government Bonds, and debentures, which offer a lower risk than equity investments. Compared to equity investments in ULIP plans, however, debt funds may offer a lower return on investment.
        As these types of funds carry low to medium risk, returns are usually not high.
      3. HYBRID/BALANCED FUNDS: Under ULIP plans, Hybrid or Balanced Funds are designed to provide capital growth (from the equity component) while ensuring lower risk (due to the debt component.) In case of market fluctuations, thus, any loss that you incur from the equity portion is balanced out by the lower risk yet consistent returns from the fund's debt portion.
      The table below enumerates the various aspects of the ULIP plan fund options
      FUND TYPE INVESTMENT
      EQUITY FUNDS Primary investments include company stocks that focus on capital appreciation
      DEBT FUNDS Investments include government securities, corporate bonds, and other fixed-income
      HYBRID/BALANCED FUNDS Investments combine equity component with fixed interest instruments

    Key Benefits

    Dual Benefit – Insurance + Investment
    1. Provides a life cover in case of the policyholder’s demise
    2. Invests a portion of the premium in market-linked funds (equity, debt, or hybrid)
    Flexibility
    1. Choose from various investment funds based on your risk appetite (aggressive, balanced, or conservative)
    2. Switch funds anytime during the policy tenure (many plans offer unlimited free switches)
    Wealth Enhancement
    1. Offers loyalty additions, wealth boosters, or return of charges to increase fund value
    2. Helps in long-term wealth creation through compounding returns
    Tax Benefits
    1. Eligible for tax deductions under Section 80C for premiums paid
    2. Maturity benefits may be tax-free under Section 10(10D) (subject to conditions)
    Insurance Benefits
  • Life cover ensures financial support to your family in case of death
    Additional Riders
    1. Critical illness cover
    2. Accidental death/disability benefits
    3. Waiver of premium
  • Goal-based protection (e.g., child education, retirement) is built into specific plans

    1. Individuals looking for a long-term investment with life protection
    2. People comfortable with market-linked returns
    3. Those planning for financial goals like children's education, wealth creation, or retirement

    It comes with (Single Pay / Limited Pay / Regular Pay)

    MAJOR FEATURES
    1. Fixed Maturity
      • Policy matures after the selected policy term.
      • Entire Fund Value is payable on maturity (unless Settlement Option is exercised).
    2. Return of Charges (RoC): One of the biggest attractions of this plan.
      Return of Charges is a unique feature that refunds all policy charges (excluding certain charges) at maturity.
      This means that the eligible charges deducted during the policy term are added back to the Fund Value at maturity, enhancing the overall returns for the policyholder.
      At maturity, eligible charges deducted during the policy term are added back to the Fund Value according to the premium band selected.
      Eligible charges include:
      • Premium Allocation Charges

      • Policy Administration Charges

      • mortality Charge (Death Benefit)
      (Extra mortality, rider charges and GST are excluded.)
    3. Guaranteed Loyalty Additions (GLA) : Starting from the end of the 8th policy year,
      Guaranteed Loyalty Additions are credited every year.
      Higher premium bands receive larger additions.
    4. Maturity Benefit: On maturity:
      Fund Value = Number of Units × Applicable NAV
      The entire fund value is paid to the policyholder.
    5. Death Benefit: In the event of the death of the life insured, the death benefit is paid to the nominee. Nominee receives the highest of:
      • Sum Assured on Death

      • Fund Value

      • Minimum Death Benefit (as per the policy terms)
    WHOLE LIFE VARIANT Provides life insurance coverage for the entire lifetime of the policyholder, along with Investment opportunities for lifelong protection and wealth creation.
    This is the flagship feature of Flexi Wealth Advantage Plan.
    Unlike normal ULIPs that mature after 10–20 years, this variant provides life cover and investment Continuity up to age 100, subject to plan terms.
    Objective : Create wealth throughout your lifetime while retaining insurance protection and the flexibility to generate a regular income later in life.
    MAJOR FEATURES
    1. Whole Life Protection
      • Life cover continues until the life insured reaches 100 years of age.
      • Death benefit is paid to the nominee in case of the life insured's demise.
        • Coverage continues until 100 years of age.
        Coverage continues until 100 years of age.You generally pay premiums only during the chosen Premium Paying Term (such as 5, 10, 12, 15 or 20 years, depending on eligibility, while the investment remains in force thereafter
    2. Smart Withdrawal Option : This feature is exclusive to the Whole Life Variant.
      It allows policyholders to receive systematic withdrawals from the accumulated Fund Value after The premium-paying term is completed.
      This option provides a steady income stream during retirement or later stages of life, while Keeping the investment intact for future growth.
      It enables systematic withdrawals from the accumulated Fund Value, making it useful for:
      • Retirement Income

      • Supplementing Pension

      • Meeting Regular Expenses

        • This allows the policy to function as a long-term income-generating asset while maintaining the remaining investment.
    3. Return of Charges (Periodic): This feature refunds all policy charges (excluding certain charges) Periodically during the policy term, enhancing the overall fund value.

      Unlike the Wealth Variant, where charges are returned only at maturity:
      In the Whole Life Variant, eligible charges are returned periodically (e.g., every 5 years), which can help boost the fund value over time and provide more liquidity for the policyholder.
      This periodic return of charges can be particularly beneficial for long-term policyholders, as it allows them to benefit from the refund of charges without having to wait until the end of the policy term. In the Whole Life Variant:
      • Charges deducted up to (PPT + 10th year) are returned at the end of that period.
      • Thereafter, charges deducted during each subsequent five-year block are returned every five years (or at maturity, if earlier)
    4. Legacy Planning: The Whole Life Variant also offers robust legacy planning features, allowing policyholders to create a lasting financial impact for their beneficiaries.

      5. Because the plan can continue until age 100:
      • The investment may continue growing over a longer period.
      • It can support retirement income and also help create a financial legacy for beneficiaries.
    5. Guaranteed Loyalty Additions: The Whole Life Variant also includes guaranteed loyalty additions, which are additional benefits provided to policyholders based on their loyalty and continued commitment to the policy.
      4GLAs begin from the 8th policy year and continue based on the premium band. For many premium bands, higher GLA rates become applicable after the (PPT + 10th year), rewarding long-term policy continuation.

    Optional Add On benefits
  • Axis Max Life Critical Illness and Disability Secure Rider (UIN: 104A034V02)2 : This rider provides benefit upon diagnosis of any of the 64 critical illnesses covered, and maybe opted at inception or anytime during the policy term, by Payment of a nominal additional premium.
  • Waiver of Premium Benefit (optional at inception)3 : This option ensures that, in case of unfortunate demise of the policyholder provided the risk cover under the Policy is in-force, WOP has been chosen at Inception and WOP cover is active on the date of death of the policyholder, the Company will fund all future outstanding premiums of the base policy only (not additional riders chosen) as and when due under the policy, keeping all the promised benefits under the policy intact. No additional premium will be required to avail this benefit. It will be deducted as a charge levied on every monthly anniversary by cancelling units from the unit account during the premium payment term of the base policy.

    Death Benefit Irrespective of whether Waiver of Premium Benefit is opted for or not opted for at inception:
    1. On the death of the Life Insured during the premium payment term, the nominee shall get the higher of the following benefits, given the Policy is in force:
    Sum Assured (Reduced by applicable partial withdrawals, if any), or
    Fund Value (as on date of intimation of death)
    2. On death of the Life Insured anytime during the term of the Policy, the nominee shall get higher of the following benefits, given the Policy is in force:
    Sum Assured (Reduced by applicable partial withdrawals, if any), or
    Single Pay It is equal to Cover multiple* X Single premium
    Limited Pay & Regular Pay It is equal to Cover multiple* X Annualised premium
    *Cover multiple options may be checked from the section “Axis Max Life Flexi Wealth Advantage Plan at a glance”
    Note: The Sum Assured on Death will be reduced by the amount of any partial withdrawals made from the Policy.
  • Fund value (as of the date of intimation of death), or
  • 105% of the Total Premiums received up to the date of death (Reduced by applicable partial withdrawals, if any)
    •  Further, if Waiver of Premium (WOP) Benefit is opted at inception and the WOP cover is active on the date of death of the policyholder:
    On the death of the policyholder, subject to the policy being in force, the company shall fund all future outstanding Premiums of the base Policy as and when due under the Policy and all committed Policy benefits shall continue as is.
    Once the WOP benefit has been accepted under your Policy and future premium(s) are being funded by the Company, then Subsequently, in case the life insured surrenders the base policy or dies, the company will pay the present value of the future premiums (if any) in addition to the other payable base benefit (Surrender Value in case of surrender and Death Benefit in case of death of life insured). The present value will be calculated at the discount rate of 6.00% p.a.
    Maturity Benefit On maturity, you will be eligible to receive an amount, provided the settlement option has not been exercised, equal to the Fund Value as applicable on the date of maturity of the policy, where the Fund Value will be calculated as:
    Fund Value = Summation of Number of Units in Fund(s) multiplied by the respective NAV of the Fund(s) as on the date of maturity
    Return of Charges (RoC) You are eligible to get back the charges deducted under your policy basis the variant and premium amount opted by You, provided all due premiums have been paid
    1. Wealth Variant: RoC basis, the charges deducted from inception till maturity will be paid on the date of maturity
    2. Whole Life Variant: RoC basis the charges deducted between inception and (PPT+10)th year will be returned at end of (PPT+10th) year. Thereafter, the RoC bases the charges deducted during the next five years will be returned at the end of every 5 years or maturity, whichever is earlier

    Smart Withdrawals You can avail this feature, if you choose the whole life variant, to systematically withdraw money from your fund value and plan a secondary income as per your need if all due premiums under your Policy have been paid. you can choose to Withdraw a predetermined percentage of the fund value from your funds regularly.
    In any particular year, the amount of smart withdrawal is equal to the chosen percentage of the fund, shall happen only if the fund value is greater than or equal to Minimum Death Benefit. The Minimum Death Benefit is defined as the higher of Sum Assured on Death and 105% of total premiums paid.
    Switch There is no limit on number of switches done in a policy year i.e., you may switch any number of times without any charges being levied.
    You may switch between available Funds at any time during the Policy Term, subject to a minimum Switch amount of ₹5,000.
    You shall not be allowed to exercise this option during the period of discontinuation in first five years of the policy. Switches will be allowed during the settlement period.
    Premium Redirect ion There is no limit on the number of premium redirections done in a Policy Year without any charges being levied. You may redirect your future premiums between available Funds at any time by giving us a written notice before the Premium due date. You will need to notify the Company of the amount/proportion of the premium to be paid into each fund at the time of redirection.
    Partial Withdrawal You can make partial withdrawals which will be affected by cancelling units subject to the following conditions
    Applicable for both the Wealth variant and the Whole Life variant
    1. No partial withdrawals are allowed in the first five Policy Years, and thereafter a maximum of twelve (12) partial withdrawals are allowed in any policy year
    2. The minimum amount of partial withdrawal allowed per transaction is ₹ 5,000

    4. Mortality Charge
    on Death Benefit    		 The mortality charge on death benefit will be levied on the basis ‘Sum at Risk’ on every monthly anniversary by canceling units from the unit account starting from the date of commencement of Policy.
    The mortality charge on death benefit will be on an attained age of the Life Insured basis over the durat ion of The contract.
    The charge is per ₹1,000 of Sum at Risk and will depend on the gender and attained age of the Life Insured
    Sum at Risk (SAR) for the death benefit is defined as follows:
    Max (Sum Assured, 105% of all premiums paid) less applicable partial withdrawals
    Total Fund Value, 0) Charge per ₹ 1,000 of Sum at Risk
    Sum at Risk (SAR) for the product during the settlement period is defined as follows:
    Max (105% of Total premiums paid – Total Fund Value, 0)
    Please note that the ‘applicable partial withdrawals’ mentioned above refer to all the partial withdrawals
    (except smart withdrawals) made during the two years’ period immediately preceding the date of calculation of sum at risk.
    5. Mortality Charge on
    Waiver of Premium

It shall stop once the Waiver of Premium benefit has been triggered.

    Unit Linked Insurance Plans Offered by
    AXIS MAX LIFE

    Axis Max Life Insurance offers certain ULIPs that combine life protection with market-linked investments. Here’s a simplified overview that will help you understand the Unit Linked Insurance Plans offered by AMLI:

    ULIP BENEFITS HOW IT WORKS SUITABLE FOR
    FLEXI WEALTH ADVANTAGE PLAN This plan focuses on long-term wealth creation with life cover. It offers multiple fund options and investment strategies The premium is split between insurance and market-linked investments. This allows switching between funds based on your goals. This plan is suitable for individuals who are looking for flexible investment strategies with insurance protectio
    FLEXI WEALTH PLUS PLAN This plan is designed for goal-based wealth creation. It offers flexibility in both investment allocation and premium payments The investments are linked to market performance. It gives you the option to adjust your funds over time as per your financial goals This plan is ideal for individuals who are planning for milestones like education, retirement, or wealth building
    FAST TRACK SUPER PLAN This plan focuses on faster wealth accumulation. It includes life cover along with market-linked growth The premium is invested in selected funds that have the potential to give higher returns over time. This plan is suitable for individuals who are looking for early financial
    Smart Term with Additional Return ULIP (STAR ULIP) This plan combines high life coverage with market-linked returns. It may also include additional protection benefits. Blends term insurance with ULIP investment. It also provides a death benefit along with investment growth. This plan is ideal for individuals who are looking for stronger protection combined with wealth creation.

    MAJOR FUNDS

    Major Funds are as follows:
    1. Axis Max Life BSE Dividend Stability Index Fund: The Axis Max Life BSE Dividend Stability Index Fund is a passively managed equity fund. It aims to invest in a basket of stocks drawn from companies listed in the BSE Dividend Stability Index. This index fund therefore primarily invests in large-cap businesses with a proven track record of high dividend payouts. Benchmarked against the BSE Dividend Stability Index, the BSE Largecap Index would serve as the stock universe for this fund. This means that the fund’s portfolio will primarily feature financially strong companies with strong cash flows that have historically offered consistent dividend payouts to its stockholders.
    2. Axis Max Life High Growth Fund: Axis Max Life High Growth Fund is an open-ended multi-cap fund that primarily invests in midcap equities of companies with high growth potential in the long term
    3. Axis Max Life UL Pure Growth Fund: Axis Max Life UL Pure Growth Fund (SFIN: ULIF02630/12/22PUREGROWTH104) is an open-ended equity-oriented scheme that does not invest in companies that draw a large portion of their income from sectors such as Banking & Financial Services, entertainment such as cinema/television, gambling, specific types of animal produce, tobacco/tobacco products and alcoholic beverages.
    4. Axis Max Life UL Life Secure Plus Fund: Axis Max Life UL Secure Plus Fund is a debt-oriented scheme focused on providing capital protection to investors. Currently investment in this scheme is allowed only under the Systematic Transfer Plan (STP) strategy
    5. Axis Max Life UL Life Conservative Fund is an open-ended hybrid fund that predominantly invests in debt instruments with equities comprising a minor portion of the investment portfolio
    6. Axis Max Life UL Life Balanced Fund :Axis Max Life UL Life Balanced Fund is an open-ended hybrid fund that invests in a mix of domestic equities and debt instruments

    BENEFITS OF ULIPS

    ULIP means an opportunity to invest in various market-related securities such as equity, debt, andbalanced funds to receive long-term investment returns. ULIP full form is Unit Linked Insurance Plans,which means your investments in funds are subject to market fluctuations. So, you can choose to investin a variety of fund options with ULIP plan, depending upon your risk appetite and investment objectives.

    1. Maturity Benefit: On maturity of the ULIP policy, you become eligible to avail of an amount equal to the accumulated fund value as a maturity/ survival benefit.
    2. Death Benefit: In case of untimely demise at any time within the ULIP policy tenure, your family will receive the ULIP insurance benefit as per the policy terms and conditions
    3. Loyalty Additions:The best ULIPs help you boost your accumulated wealth through loyalty additions, at the end of each policy year. A specific percentage of the fund value under the ULIP is added to your policy earnings through the creation of additional units. Loyalty Additions are offered under the following plans by Axis Max Life Insurance.
    4. Future Goal PlanningULIPs can help achieve long-term financial goals, such as a child's education, marriage, retirement planning, wealth creation, or buying a house. Since the returns from ULIPs are market-linked, they yield best when held for a long-term duration. Such plans also come with a mandatory 5-year lock-in period, which encourages goal-oriented, disciplined investing. In fact, ULIPs can be an ideal investment for future goal achievement, given the features like flexibility, tax benefits, and professional fund managers’ involvement.
    5. Market Linked Returns: ULIP means an opportunity to avail market-linked returns by allocating a portion of the premium invested into market-linked instruments such as debt and equity instruments (in varying proportions)
    6. Life Protection with Investment: Besides allocating a portion of the premium invested into market-linked instruments, Unit linked Insurance plans provide life cover.
      Thus, you can avail market-linked returns, while the ULIP plan takes care of your protection needs.
      With the need of protection against life's eventualities out of the way, you can develop a regular habit of saving and investing and build substantial wealth over the long term with ULIP plans.
    7. Benefit of Life Cover and Investment: This is the core strength of a ULIP. It delivers both life cover and wealth creation under a single plan. In the event of your demise within the policy period, your nominee typically receives the higher of the sum assured or the accumulated fund value. If you survive the policy term, you get the fund value at maturity.
    8. Freedom of Investment Choices :ULIPs offer significant flexibility in how your money is invested. You can choose from a range of funds based on your risk appetite and goals. Most plans allow you to switch between funds as market conditions or your life stages change.
    9. Protection Against Financial Uncertainty : ULIPs provide a safety net for your family against various unexpected future events like the life insured’s untimely demise or diagnosis of critical illness. The life cover benefit of a ULIP plan ensures financial protection through a lump sum payout to nominee. It helps them manage financial responsibilities such as loans, education, or daily expenses.
    10. Tax Benefits: Save More with ULIPs:ULIPs are among the few products that offer tax benefit at different stages of its investment cycle. Tax benefits of ULIPs start from the initial investment, continue while you stay invested and are even applicable at the time of exit/maturity. This makes them tax-efficient for long-term wealth building. The premiums paid offer the benefit of tax deduction and maturity/death benefits may also be tax exempt subject to applicable terms and conditions.
    11. . How ULIP Helps You Save on Taxes?: ULIP helps you save tax in several different ways under the Income Tax Act, 2025. Here are a few ways mentioned:
      • ENTRY: You can claim a deduction up to ₹1.5 lakh per financial year on premiums paid, subject to the overall Section 123 limit and policy conditions.
      • GROWTH: Fund switches are generally not taxable events
      • EXIT: Under Section 11 (read with Schedule II, Sr. No. 2), qualifying maturity and death benefits can be tax exempt subject to applicable terms and conditions

    RIDERS IN AXIS MAX LIFE

    RIDERS are additional benefits that can be added to a base insurance policy to enhance coverage. Axis Max Life offers a variety of riders that provide extra protection and financial support in case of specific events or conditions.
    Riders in life insurance are optional add-on benefits that can be attached to a base policy by paying an additional premium. They help customise the policy according to specific risks such as critical illness, disability, accidental death, or premium-payment difficulties.
    Here are some of the key riders available with Axis Max Life policies:

    Why Riders Are Important

    Riders are important because they allow policyholders to tailor their insurance coverage to better suit their specific needs and circumstances. They provide additional financial protection against risks that may not be covered by the base policy, ensuring that the policyholder and their family are better prepared for unforeseen events. By adding riders, policyholders can enhance the value of their insurance plan and have peace of mind knowing that they have comprehensive coverage for a wider range of situations.
    A basic life insurance policy primarily covers death. However, many financial risks occur during your lifetime, such as:

  • Critical illnesses (e.g., cancer, heart attack, stroke etc)
  • Disability (temporary or permanent)
  • Accidental death
  • Inability to pay premiums due to job loss or disability
  • Hospitalization expenses
  • Income loss due to death or disability
  • Long-term care needs
  • Other specific risks based on your lifestyle or family history
    •

    Riders help bridge these protection gaps. They allow you to customize your insurance plan to better match your life stage, health profile, and financial goals. By adding riders, you can ensure that you have comprehensive coverage that addresses a wider range of risks, providing greater financial security for you and your loved ones.

    1. Critical Illness Rider: This rider provides a lump sum benefit if the policyholder is diagnosed with a specified critical illness such as cancer, heart attack, stroke, etc. It helps cover medical expenses and provides financial support during a difficult time.
    2. Waiver of Premium Rider: If the policyholder becomes disabled or unable to work due to an accident or illness, this rider waives off future premium payments while keeping the policy active. It ensures that the coverage continues without any financial burden on the policyholder.
    3. Accidental Death Benefit Rider: This rider provides an additional payout in case of accidental death. It offers extra financial security to the family of the policyholder in the unfortunate event of an accident.
    4. Income Benefit Rider: In case of the policyholder's death, this rider provides a regular income to the nominee for a specified period. It helps maintain financial stability for the family after the loss of the primary breadwinner.
    5. Hospital Cash Rider: This rider provides a daily cash benefit for each day the policyholder is hospitalized due to illness or injury. It helps cover additional expenses incurred during hospital stays, such as transportation, food, and other non-medical costs.

    Axis Max Life Critical Illness
    & Disability Secure Rider (CIDSR)

    Axis Max Life's Critical Illness & Disability Secure Rider (CIDSR) is a comprehensive rider that provides financial protection in case of critical illness diagnosis or disability. It offers a lump sum benefit upon diagnosis of specified critical illnesses or in the event of permanent disability, helping policyholders manage medical expenses and maintain financial stability during challenging times.
    This rider provides a lump-sum payout if the insured is diagnosed with any covered critical illness or suffers total and permanent disability.
    Investment in your health is one of the best kind of investment. With that understanding, Axis Max Life brings you a comprehensive plan that covers you against the uncertainties that life has to offer.
    Axis Max Life Critical Illness and Disability Rider provides you the following main benefits:

  • Comprehensive CI cover: Option to choose Gold variant (coverage of 22 CI) or Platinum variant (coverage of 64 CI)
  • Total and Permanent Disability variant: This rider offers coverage on Total and Permanent Disability
  • Flexible payment option: You can opt for limited pay or regular pay option as per your base plan for the rider cover
  • Max Fit Program: A Wellness Benefit is available in this rider with the objective of maintaining customer’s good health and improving customer engagement. The program includes health risk assessment, personalized health tips, and rewards for healthy behaviors.
  • Critical Illness Benefit: If the insured is diagnosed with any of the specified critical illnesses (such as cancer, heart attack, stroke, etc.), a lump sum benefit is paid out to help cover medical expenses and provide financial support during treatment and recovery.
  • Disability Benefit: In the event of total and permanent disability due to an accident or illness, this rider provides a lump sum payout to assist with ongoing care, rehabilitation, and lifestyle adjustments required due to the disability.

    The Rider Policy Term cannot be higher than base plan Policy Term
    Premium Payment Terms & Policy Term Premium Payment Term can be same as Policy Term or less than Policy Term. The Rider Policy Term cannot be higher than base plan Policy Term
    LIMITED PAY
    (PPT < PT)    		 5 to 19 Years (PPT plus 1) to 20 Years
    Regular Pay
    (PPT = PT)    		 5 to 20 Years 5 to 20 Years
    Available Rider Policy Term shall be subject to applicable maximum maturity age.
    A policyholder can choose to attach the rider any time during the subsequent policy anniversary as per the available rider terms and conditions.
    The Rider Premium Payment Term cannot be higher than base plan Premium Payment Term
    Premium Payment modes The premium payment mode and modal factor for the rider are the same as under the base policy
    Minimum Sum Assured Minimum initial Rider Sum Assured is ₹ 1,00,000
    Rider Sum Assured (Rider SA) is equal to “sum assured under heath cover”
    "Sum assured under health cover" means an absolute amount of benefit which is guaranteed to become payable on happening of insured health related contingency in accordance with the terms and conditions of the policy under health cover
    Maximum Sum Assured Maximum initial Rider Sum Assured is ₹ 1,00,00,000
    The maximum initial Rider Sum Assured that can be opted for is ₹ 1 crore.
    The maximum initial Rider SA as a proportion of Sum Assured under the base product will be as per the prevailing regulations. The Rider sum assured cannot exceed the sum assured under the base product.
    In case, the insured has option to reduce Sum Assured under base plan and if such reduced Sum Assured is less than the rider Sum Assured, the rider SA shall automatically reduce to comply with the regulation
    Minimum Annualised Premium Minimum annualised premium for the rider is ₹ 1,000
    As per minimum rider sum assured and minimum premium rate, the minimum annualised premium for the rider is ₹ 1,000.
    The minimum annualised premium for the rider is subject to the prevailing regulations and may vary based on the rider variant chosen.
    Maximum Annualised Premium As per maximum rider sum assured, subjected to board approved underwriting policy of the company.
    In addition, note that the premium pertaining to health related or critical illness riders shall not exceed 100% of premium under the basic product, the premiums under all other life insurance riders put together shall not exceed 30% of premiums under the basic product.
    All applicable taxes, cesses and levies are collected over and above the rider premium.
    Product to which the rider will be attached The rider can be attached to the following base products of Axis Max Life Insurance Company Limited:
    1. Axis Max Life Savings Advantage Plan

    9. Axis Max Life Smart Total Elite Protection Plan
    As this rider is an additional benefit rider, both the base benefit and the rider benefit will be paid, even if there is an overlap. Hence there shall be no overlap in benefit offered under riders & different base products.
    Coverage Gold variant (22 critical illnesses) or Platinum variant (64 critical illnesses)
    Disability Coverage Covers total and permanent disability due to accident or illness
    Payment Flexibility Option for limited pay or regular pay based on the base plan
    Wellness Program Includes health risk assessment, personalized health tips, and rewards for healthy behaviors

    Total and Permanent Disability Benefit (TPDB)

    In the event of total and permanent disability due to an accident or illness, this rider provides a lump sum payout to assist with ongoing care, rehabilitation, and lifestyle adjustments required due to the disability.
    Total and Permanent Disability (TPD) is a condition where an individual is unable to perform any work or occupation for a continuous period of at least 6 months due to an accident or illness. The Total and Permanent Disability Benefit (TPDB) provides financial support to the insured in such cases by paying out a lump sum amount. This benefit helps the insured manage medical expenses, rehabilitation costs, and lifestyle adjustments required due to the disability, ensuring financial stability during challenging times.
    TPD shall mean the occurrence of any of the following conditions as a result of accidental bodily injury, sickness or disease:

    1. Permanent Disability: Disability means inability of the Insured Person to perform at least 3 of the 6 activities of daily living as listed below (either with or without the use of mechanical equipment, special devices or other aids and adaptations in use for disabled persons) for a continuous period of at least 6 months:
    2. Physical Impairment
      1. Total and irrecoverable loss of sight of both eyes. The blindness must be confirmed by an Ophthalmologist, OR
      2. Loss of use or loss by severance of two or more limbs at or above wrists or ankles; OR
      3. The total and irrecoverable loss of sight of one eye and loss of use or loss by severance of one limb at or above wrist or ankle.

        4. The above disability must have lasted, without interruption, for at least six consecutive months from the date of diagnosis or accident and must, in the opinion of a qualified medical practitioner appointed by the Company, be deemed permanent.

    3. Accident means sudden, unforeseen and involuntary event caused by external, visible and violent mean
    4. Accidental Injury means bodily injury of the insured caused solely, directly and independently of any other intervening causes from an accident {i.e. a traumatic event of violent, unexpected, external and visible nature). The loss of use of a limb is considered as a loss of use when such loss of use involves total and permanent loss of function of the limb affected as determined by a registered medical practitioner nominated by the Company.
    5. Illness means a sickness or a disease or pathological condition leading to the impairment of normal physiological function which manifests itself during the policy term and requires medical treatment.

    Exclusions of TPD:

    TPD arising directly or indirectly from any of the following are specifically excluded: Axis Max Life is not be liable to make any payment under this Policy towards the TPD benefit, directly or indirectly caused by, based on, arising out of or howsoever attributable to any of the following
    TPD benefit shall not be payable in the event of disability caused directly or indirectly, wholly or partly, by any of the following:

    1. Pre-existing condition means any condition, aliment, injury or disease / critical illness / disability
      1. That is/are diagnosed by a physician within 36 months prior to the effective date of the policy issued by the insurer or its reinstatement; or
      2. For which medical advice or treatment was recommended by, or received from, a Physician within 36 months Prior to the effective date of the policy issued by the insurer or its reinstatement.

      Coverage under the policy after the expiry of 36 months for any pre-existing disease is subject to the same being declared at the time of application and accepted by Insurer

    2. Any disability directly or indirectly caused due to treatment for, Alcoholism, drug or substance abuse or any addictive condition and consequences thereof
    3. Narcotics used by the Insured Person unless taken as prescribed by a registered Medical Practitioner
    4. Any disability directly or indirectly caused due to intentional self-injury, suicide or attempted suicide, whether the person is medically sane or insane.
    5. Any disability directly or indirectly, caused by or arising from or attributable to a foreign invasion, act of foreign enemies, hostilities, warlike operations (whether war be declared or not or while performing duties in the armed forces of any country during war or at peace time), civil war, public defense, rebellion, revolution, insurrection, military or usurped power
    6. Service in any military, air-force, naval, paramilitary or similar organization
    7. Any disability caused by ionizing radiation or contamination by radioactivity from any nuclear fuel (explosive or hazardous form) or from any nuclear waste from the combustion of nuclear fuel, nuclear, chemical or biological attack.
    8. Working in underground mines, tunneling or involving electrical installations with high tension supply, or as race jockeys or circus personnel.
    9. Congenital External Anomalies, inherited disorders or any complications or conditions arising therefrom including any developmental conditions of the Insured.
    10. Any disability directly or indirectly caused by any treatment necessitated due to participation as a professional in hazardous or adventure sport, including but not limited to, para jumping rock climbing, mountaineering, rafting, motor racing, horse racing or scuba diving, hand gliding, sky diving, deep sea diving and selfie accidents
    11. Participation by the Insured Person in any flying activity, except as a bona fide, fare-paying passenger of a recognized airline on regular routes and on a scheduled timetable
    12. Any disability directly or indirectly, caused by Medical treatment traceable to childbirth (including complicated deliveries and caesarean sections incurred during hospitalization) except ectopic pregnancy. Any disability due to miscarriages (unless due to an accident) and lawful medical termination of pregnancy during the policy period.
    13. Any disability directly or indirectly, caused by any unproven / experimental treatment, service and supplies for or in connection with any treatment. Unproven / experimental treatments are treatments, procedures or supplies that lack significant medical documentation to support their effectiveness.
    14. Any disability based on certification/diagnosis/treatment from persons not registered as Medical Practitioners, or from a Medical Practitioner who is practicing outside the discipline that he/ she is licensed for
    15. Any disability directly or indirectly, caused due to any treatment, including surgical management, to change characteristics of the body to those of opposite sex
    16. Any disability directly or indirectly, caused due to cosmetic or plastic surgery or any treatment to change the appearance unless for reconstruction following an Accident, Burn(s), or Cancer or as part of medically necessary treatment to remove a direct and immediate health risk to the insured. For this to be considered a medical necessity, it must be certified by the attending Medical Practitioner.
    17. Any disability directly or indirectly, caused due to surgical treatment of obesity that does not fulfil all the below conditions
      1. Surgery to be conducted is upon the advice of the Doctor
      2. The Surgery / Procedure conducted should be supported by clinical protocols
      3. The member has to be 18 years of age or older and
      4. Body Mass Index (BMI) of 40 or more, or BMI of 35 or more with one or more obesity related complications.
      5. Obesity related cardiomyopathy
      6. Coronary heart disease (CHD)
      7. Type 2 diabetes mellitus with target organ damage despite optimal therapy
      8. Severe Sleep Apnea
        9.
    18. Any disability directly or indirectly, caused due to treatments received in health hydros, nature cure clinics, spas or similar establishments or private beds registered as a nursing home attached to such establishments or where admission is arranged wholly or partly for domestic reason.
    19. Any disability directly or indirectly, caused by treatment directly arising from or consequent upon any Insured Person committing or attempting to commit a breach of law with criminal intent
    20. In the event of the death of the Insured Person within the stipulated survival period as set out above.
    21. Any disability directly or indirectly, caused by sterility and infertility. This includes
      1. Any treatment related to sterility and infertility including any complication arising out of such treatment
      2. Assisted Reproductive services including artificial insemination and advanced reproductive technologies such as IVF, ZIFT, GIFT, ICSI.
      3. Gestational Surrogacy
      4. Reversal of sterilization

    WAIVER OF PREMIUM (WOP)

    The Waiver of Premium Plus Rider ensures that if a specified unfortunate event happens to the policyholder, all future premiums of the base policy and attached riders are waived, while the policy benefits continue

    FEATURES WAIVER OF PREMIUM (WOP)
    Type of Rider A Non - Linked Non - Participating Individual Pure Risk Health Insurance Rider
    Coverage All individuals in accordance with Board approved underwriting policy of the Company
    Age at Entry Minimum: 18 years; Maximum: 65 years
    Maximum Maturity Age On Policy Anniversary coinciding with or immediately following the Policyholder
    attaining age of 70 years
    Rider Benefit Rider provides waiver for all future premiums under a policy and all other attaching Riders
    on earlier happening of either of the following events,
    provided the base policy and attaching Riders are in force
    1. Critical Illness
    2. Dismemberment
    3. Death (only when Life Insured and Policyholder are different individuals
      4. Once the claim under this Rider is accepted and future premium(s) are waived, then in case of
      termination of base policy due to happening of any insured event or surrender
      (only if Surrender Value is available under the base policy),
      the present value of future premiums (if any) to be waived will be paid
      in addition to benefits under the base policy.
      The present value will be calculated at discount rate of 6.50%
    What is Covered 11 Critical Illnesses are Covered:
    1. Cancer
    2. First Heart Attack
    3. Open chest CABG
    4. Open heart replacement or repair of heart valves
    5. Kidney failure
    6. Coma
    7. Stroke
    8. Major organ / bone marrow transplant
    9. Permanent paralysis of limbs
    10. Motor neuron disease
    11. Multiple sclerosis

    Dismemberment: Dismemberment is defined as any of the following impairments
    due to illness or injury

  • Total and irrecoverable loss of entire sight in both eyes
  • Amputation or loss of use, of both hands at or above the wrists
  • Amputation or loss of use, of both feet at or above the ankles
  • Amputation or loss of use, of one hand at or above the wrist and one foot at or above the ankle
    • In order for a benefit to be payable, such dismemberment must have persisted continuously for a period
    of at least 180 days and must, in the opinion of a suitable medical practitioner,
    appointed by the Company, be deemed permanent
    Rider Term Minimum Rider Term: 2 years However, the Rider Coverage Term cannot be higher than remaining Premium Payment Term of the base plan.
    Maximum Rider Term: 30 years, subject to Policyholder not exceeding age 70 years (last birthday). However, the Rider Coverage Term cannot be higher than remaining Premium Payment Term of the base plan
    Premium Payment Term Same as the Rider Policy Term
    Premium Payment Mode The Premium Payment Mode will be same as base plan
    Maximum Sum at Risk The maximum sum at risk amount is determined basis maximum annual premium of base plan along with attaching riders (if any) of ₹25,00,000.
    Maximum Rider Premium The Maximum Rider Premium will be calculated basis the maximum base plan premium to which the Rider is attached. However, the premium pertaining to health related or critical illness riders shall not exceed 100% of premium under the base plan, and any benefit arising under the captioned rider shall not exceed the sum assured under the base plan
    Lapse and Revival If the Rider Premium or the Premium under the base Policy is not received by the expiry of the applicable Grace Period which results in the Rider or the base Policy or both lapsing or going into non-forfeiture mode, the Rider will automatically lapse and no benefits will be payable under the Rider on the occurrence of the insured event or otherwise unless the Rider is revived. Revival of the rider will be same as the base plan
    Termination of Rider This Rider shall terminate upon the happening of the first of the following events:
  • On the date of receipt of free-look cancellation request
  • On acceptance of the claim under this Ride
  • On the date of intimation of repudiation of the claim in accordance with the provisions of this Rider (only in case of death of the Policyholder)
  • On the expiry of the Revival Period
  • On the expiry of the Rider Term
  • On the maturity of the base policy or the date on which the base policy is surrendered, terminated or cancelled for any reason
  • On the expiry of the Premium Payment Term under the base policy
  • On receipt of written request for cancellation of this Rider, effective from the next Rider Premium due date
  • On cancellation / termination of this rider on grounds of misrepresentation, fraud or non-disclosure
  • On the Policy Anniversary on which the Policyholder attains the age of 70 years
    •

    How This Rider Works

    R is 35 years old, is married to Rita who is 32 years old and are blessed with a baby girl, A. In order to plan for his financial security and create a corpus for Avni’s highler education, Rajiv buys Axis Max Life Smart Wealth Advantage Growth Par Plan (Non-Linked Participating Individual Life Insurance Savings Plan (Base Product), chooses Future Income variant with a Policy Term of 35 years and Premium Payment Term of 10 years, and an Annual Premium of Rs. 1,00,000.
    However he is worried about Avni’s future in case he suffers from any eventuality.
    He opts for Axis Max Life Waiver of Premium Plus Rider which will ensure that in case he is diagnosed with critical illnesses or is disabled due to any reason, the policy continues without requiring any future premium payment and ensure all future benefits remain intact.

  • Annualised Premium: Smart Wealth Advantage Growth Par Plan-Rs. 1,00,000 p.a.
  • Axis Max Life Waiver of Premium Plus Rider – Rs. 1,470

    • In Sixth Policy Year Rajiv meets with an Accident and loses both his arm
    All his future premiums are waived off under Axis Max Life Waiver of Premium Plus Rider and policy continues
    Total Maturity benefit:

  • @4% - Rs. 21,12,500
  • @8% - Rs. 38,85,400
    •

    Accidental Death and Dismemberment Rider

    In the unfortunate event of the policyholder's death or dismemberment due to an accident, this rider provides a lump sum payout to the insured's beneficiaries, offering financial support during a difficult time.
    life is full of uncertainties and you certainly don’t want an accident to make a dent in your financial planning. We, at Axis Max Life Insurance, understand this, which is why we offer you a rider to make your financial protection planning comprehensive.
    You can add Axis Max Life Accidental Death and Dismemberment Rider to your life insurance policy (at any time, provided the remaining term of the base policy is at least 5 years) to provide additional protection benefits in case you meet with an accident, leading to dismemberment or death. The benefits under this rider are payable over and above the base plan benefits
